拘置所への道を、ぽつぽつと歩く。
Walking bit by bit, on the road towards the prison.

義侠心溢れるジャーナリストを殺めた行為は両肩に重かった。　罪――何処かへ捨てることも、誰かに預けることも、決して叶わない荷。
The act of killing a chivalrous journalist was a heavy weight on one's shoulders. Sin -- Even if you throw it away somewhere, or leave it to someone else, it is an unbearable burden.

生き続ける限りそれは積み重ねられ続ける。だからこそ人は正しく生きて少しでも荷を減らすのだ。　が、この俺はあたかも精神の剛力を誇示するが如く、殺人という最大の罪を次から次へと抱え込んでいる。
It keeps accumulating for as long as you live. That is why people try to live correctly to decrease that burden wherever possible. However, as I put my spiritual strength on display, I find myself being saddled with the greatest sin of murder one after another.

銀星号を止める、その自己一身の欲求のためだけに。
Stopping the Silver Star, just because of that selfish desire.

……俺は愚かなのだろう。　おそらく、最も質の悪い意味で愚かなのだ。
...I'm stupid. Perhaps, even foolish in the worst possible sense.

嘲笑うにも値しない。　唾棄する以外に仕様もない、愚物。　　そうと自覚してなお続ける、救いの無さ。
Not even worth laughing at. A fool, worthless aside from being the target of disdain. There is no salvation, so I kept going even after coming to that realization.

《……御堂》
《...Midou》

「…………」
「…………」

《繰り返し、言ってきたことだけれどね。　貴方は何も考えなくていい》
《I've said this time and time again. You don't have to think about anything.》

《私に使われていればいい。心を止めて。　止められないなら……私を憎めばいい》
《Just let yourself be used by me. Stop thinking about it. If you can't stop... just hate me.》

《……自分を憎むのはやめて……》
《...Stop hating yourself...》

「俺の答えも、繰り返し言ってきた」
「I've also told you my answer, time and time again.」

《……》
《……》

「劒冑は道具だ。　使われるものに過ぎない」
「A Tsurugi is a tool. It is merely something to be used.」

「使われるだけの道具は罪など背負えない。　使う人間が罪を背負う」
「A tool that is only meant to be used cannot carry the burden of sin. The person who uses them bears it.」

「憎悪に値するのは人間のみだ。　分際を知れ、道具」
「Only humans deserve hatred. Know your place, tool.」

《…………》
《…………》

同様の対話を幾度交わしたろう。　二年前のあの時、村正と結縁してから。
We've had this same discussion multiple times already. Two years ago, at that time, ever since I've made a connection with Muramasa.

今のように村正が言い出すこともあれば、俺の側が口火を切ることもあった。　然して結末は毎回変わらず。二人共に黙り込んで、互いに譲らないまま話を終える。
Just like now, when Muramasa has something to say, there was also a time where I had to start the conversation. And then the result would always be the same. Both of us would be silent, and the conversation would end with neither side yielding.

俺が譲らないのは、それが譲れない部分だからだ。　村正にとっても、同じなのだろう。
When I'm not backing down, it's usually because it's something I can't give up on. I think for Muramasa, it's the same.

だから対話はいつも不毛に、相互の拒絶で終結するほかない。
That is why our conversations are always fruitless, there's no way but to end it with mutual rejection.

「だが」
「But」

《……えっ？》
《...Huh?》

「――――」
「――――」

不意に口をついて出た、逆接の一語。　そして続けるべき言葉は――
Something unexpected came out of his mouth, that one word. And then, the words that came after that were――

元通りに口を噤んで、歩く。　村正も、夜陰に潜んで従いてくる。
He went back to his usual silence, and walked. Muramasa too, concealed herself in the shade of the night and followed.

が、劒冑の沈黙は、物問いたげな成分を含んでいた。　それはそうだ。やにわに約束事を崩されれば、疑問も湧くだろう。
However, the Tsurugi's silence was interrogative in nature. Well of course. If a promise is suddenly broken, doubts will arise.

俺自身さえ不思議だった。　魔が差したかのような一刹那、俺は何を思い、何と言い募ろうとしたのか。
Even I was being strange. It was a moment that felt like I was being possessed by an evil spirit, what was I thinking, what was I trying to argue about so vehemently.

〝だが〟　　　その言葉の後に、何を。
"But"  After that word, what comes next?

既に手放してしまったそれは、もう俺の精神の沼の底だ。見えないし、手に取ることもできない。　やがては完全に溶けて、消えてしまうだろう。
I've already let that go, it's already at the bottom of the swamp within my spirit. I can't see it, and I can't grasp it. Before long it will completely melt, and disappear.

そうなって、何が不味いということも無かろうに。　俺はどうしてか、脳裏で糸を手繰っていた。
And then, it will seem as if nothing bad has happened. But for some reason, I find myself retracing a thread inside my mind.

沼の底の何かと繋がっている糸を。
A thread that is connected to the bottom of the swamp.

……言うなれば、その糸は情景だった。　但し、俺自身に根差すものとは違う。
...To put it into words, the thread was a scene. However, the one rooted within me is different.

青江の幻覚世界に囚われている最中、意識野を通り抜けていった光陰。　あれもやはり、青江の陰義で引き出されたものだったのだろう。俺の心ではない処から。
It was when I was trapped in Aoe's illusion world, that time when I was going through my own conciousness. That too, must have been something that was drawn out by Aoe's Shinogi. From a place other than my heart.

俺の夢、俺の過去に符合しない異質なそれを、俺は見た瞬間に忘却してしまったらしい。　　……どういう次第でか、今の俺は取り戻している。
I had a dream, one that didn't match my past, I immediately forgot about it the moment I saw it. ...But for some reason, I am regaining that memory.

確かに見たことを、一度忘れ去ったことをも自覚し、そして内容を思い出している。
I've realized the fact, that I had once forgotten what I saw, and that I'm now remembering its content. 

断片的にだが。　心裡の鏡面へ映し出せる。
Although it's only fragments. I can project it on the surface of my mind.

それを――――
And that――――

天と地で、争いが繰り広げられていた。　血で血を洗う――屍山を築くという表現がまさしく相応しい。
On heaven and earth, conflict was about to ensue. Wash off blood with blood―― A fitting phrase representing the piling mountain of corpses.

地上では、射手が矢を射かけ、敵陣に間隙を穿つや、騎馬の将帥率いる兵の群れが長物を連ねて押し進む。　天空では、互いを好敵と見定めた武者同士が名乗り合い、雲を裂き風に乗って、激しく太刀を打ち交わす。
Atop the earth, archers shoot their arrows, piercing through the enemy's lines, a group of soldiers led by a commander riding on horseback were lined up in a long line and kept advancing. Up on the heavens, Mushas who have ascertained one another as great adversaries named themselves, split the clouds while riding upon the winds, and violently exchanged blows with their long swords.

戦争の光景だ。　中世……そう呼ばれる時代の。
It's a scene of war. In an era known as... the Middle Ages.

詳細に観察すれば、より正確な区分も可能だった。　劒冑の形状、武者の戦闘形式、歩兵の武器装束――それらはこの戦争が源平合戦でも戦国大名の抗争でもないことを如実に語っている。
If it was observed in detail, a more accurate classification of things would be possible. The shape of the Tsurugis,  the Mushas' fighting methods, the infantries' weapons and equipment―― they were vivid depictions that tells the story of the war that was neither the Genpei War nor disputes between Daimyos of the Warring States.

何よりも、戦場に散見する旗……　赤地に金で日輪を描いた豪奢な錦織。
Above all, the flags that were scattered across the battlefield... luxurious red brocades with a golden sun drawn on them. 

それが、どちらの陣営にも存在する。　そんな事態、そんな戦争が起きた時代は、大和史上にも稀であった。
That flag, it existed on both factions. Such a situation, a time where such a war could occur, it was rare even in the history of ancient Japan.

「御父」
「Father」

傍らの声に、俺の首が独りでにそちらへ向く。
There was a voice beside me, my neck automatically turned towards it as a result.

小柄な蝦夷の女性だった。　その顔を隣から見上げる――見上げている。つまり俺の背は彼女よりも低かった。
It was a petite Emishi woman. I looked up at her face that was beside me―― I'm looking up at her face. In other words, my height was shorter than her's.
*The Emishi or Ebisu constituted a group of people who lived in northeastern Honshū in the Tōhoku region (http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emishi?oldid=494314297)

彼女が声を投じたのは俺にではない。　前方に立つ、男の背へ向けていた。
The one she was calling out to wasn't me. It was pointed towards a man who stood in front of her.

「流れが、見えたか」
「Do you see where things are going?」

「吾が方の負けであろう」
「It's going to be my lost.」

「そうさな。　……佐々木めがまたしても得意の寝返りを打ちおった」
「I guess so. ...That Sasaki double-crossed us again, which is something he's good at.」

忌々しげな男の声。　それを聞いて、俺も気付いた。
The voice of an annoying man. After hearing that, even I could tell. 

一隊が鉾の向きを逆さにし、先刻までの仲間に攻め掛かっている……。
The party had their spears turned upside down, and they were attacking their ally up until a short while ago...

「どうにもならぬ」
「There's nothing we can do about it.」

「飽間様も、支え切れぬようだ」
「It seems even Akima-sama is unable to support it.」

「……」
「……」

「あの方の赤心忠義も、佐々木の裏切り根性には敵わぬか」
「That person's devotion and loyalty is at odds with Sasaki's treacherous nature.」

「左様なことはない！」
「That's not true！」

「現に敗れている……」
「He is very down because of it...」

「一時の事だ。　うてらが奉ずる吉野の主上こそ正当の帝、いま京に御座すは尊き血筋ではあれど僭帝に過ぎぬ」
「It's only temporary. The lord of Yoshino who we serve is the true emperor, and the one who is seated in Kyoto right now is merely a tyrant, even if he is of noble blood.

「最後には正しき者が勝つ。　世は、そう出来ている」
「The one who is just will be victorious in the end. The world, it is made that way.」

「……」
「……」

「信じられぬか」
「Do you not believe?」

「信じられぬ」
「I can't believe.」

「信じねばならぬ」
「You have to.」

「吾が信ずるは、天上天下に御父のみよ」
「Throughout heaven and earth, the only one who I can believe is only Father.」

「……」
「……」

「御父に教えられた鍛冶の技を信じている。　御父がこれから見つけ出す、劒冑の極みも信じようぞ」
「I believe in the smithing skills that Father taught me. I will also believe, believe in the peak of the Tsurugi's power that Father will find.」

「そうして、御父の跡を継ぐ。　それだけが、吾の天命と思うている」
「And then, I will follow in Father's footsteps. I think only that, is my life's destiny.」

「……そうか」
「...I see.」

「帰ろう、御父。　戦は終わりだ」
「Let's go home, Father. The battle is over.」

「うむ……」
「Yes...」

「おわり？」
「Over?」

不意に、俺は声を発した。　俺のものではない声で。
Without realizing, I had let out my voice. With a voice that isn't mine.

我が身から生じる異質な声を聴く……　　それはしかし、良く慣れ親しんだ感覚だった。
I heard that the voice I produced was different... However, it felt familiar.

装甲する都度、これと同じ体験をしている。　ただ今の声は、いつもと比べると、些か幼かった。
Every time I was armouring up, I feel like it's the same experience as this.  It's just that the voice just now, it felt a little bit younger.

「かかさま。いくさ、おわったの？　もう、やらない？」
「Mother. The war, is it over? Are you not, battling anymore?」

「……」
「……」

「……」
「……」

ニュアンスの齟齬は、部外者である俺の耳にも明白だった。　幼い声の主――俺の良く知る者――は、二人の会話を誤解している。
Even to an outsider's ears like mine, the discrepancy of the nuances were evident. A lord with a young child's voice―― the things that I knew―― all of them , they're making me misunderstand the two's conversation.

女性の方が、小さく首を振った。
The woman turned her small neck. 

「まだだ。　まだ、続く」
「Not yet. It still continues.」

「いつまで？」
「For how much longer?」

「わからぬ」
「I don't know.」

「……いくさは、いつからしてるの？」
「...The war, when did it start?」

「なれの生まれる前から、ずっとだ」
「A long time ago, before you were even born.」

「あてのうまれるまえ？」
「Before I was born?」

「そうだ」
「That's right.」

「かかさまは？　かかさまのうまれたころは？」
「How about mother? How about when mother was born?」

「いくさ、なかった？」
「Was there, no war?」

「……あった」
「...There was.」

「じじさまは？」
「How about grandfather?」

「……」
「……」

「じじさまのうまれたころは？　いくさ、なかった？」
「How about when grandfather was born? Was there, no war?」

「……」
「……」

「あったよ」
「There was.」

その戦嵐は、百年に渡って大和全土を吹き荒れたと伝えられている。
It was told that the storm of war had swept over the whole land of ancient Japan for a hundred years.

南北朝争乱。　　俺の劒冑――村正が、生きていた世界。
The conflict of the Northern and Southern Courts (Nanboku-chō period). The world where my Tsurugi―― Muramasa, lived.

「御父。　飽間様がお越しだ」
「Father. Akima-sama has come.」

「おう」
「Yeah.」

鄙びた蝦夷村の素朴な屋敷。　そこに現れたのは、堂々たる風情の武人だった。
A rustic residence in a rural village in Ezo. The one who appeared there, was a warrior who had a majestic air about him.
*(Ezo is a Japanese name which historically referred to the lands to the north of Japan.)

一郡一軍を預かる将領に違いない。　一介の蝦夷とは天と地ほどの身分差がある……筈だが、家主は立ち上がりもせず、挨拶らしき挨拶もしなかった。
He was without a doubt a general who was entrusted with the area and its armies. The gap between him and a mere Emishi was like heaven and earth... that's how it's supposed to be, but the owner of the house did not stand up, nor extended his greetings.

武人に、それを不快がる気色はない。　……そういう間柄なのか。
The warrior did not show any signs of displeasure. ...Maybe they have a special relationship.

「無事で、何よりだ」
「It's great that you are safe.」

「見ていたか」
「Did you see?」

「うむ」
「Yes.」

「佐々木も大した奴よ。　裏切る時と場所を決して間違えん」
「Sasaki is truly something. There were absolutely no mistakes in the timing and place of his betrayal.」

「吉野山の方々は位階くらい気前良くくれてやるべきだった。　奴の訴えを聞き流していたばかりに、このざまだ」
「The people from Mt. Yoshino should have been more generous when it comes to court ranks. They didn't listen to his complaints, and look what happened.」

「欲得ずくの輩など要るまい。　どうせ寝返る男なら、最初から敵に回しておいた方がましだ」
「There is no use for such a calculating ally. If he is someone who will betray you, it would be better to make an enemy out of him from the beginning.」

「……あれはあれで筋は通しているがな。　領地を求め官位を求め、北から南南から北へと忙しく立ち回るのも、一族を守るためだ」
「...Even so, it does make sense. The reason why he demands to be given territory and an official rank, why he is so busy going back and forth between North and South, it was all to protect his clan.」

「本末転倒であろう。　将ならば、大義を守護するために一族の力を用いるべき」
「He has his priorities backwards. If he is a general, he should have utilized his clan's power to uphold justice.」

「一族を守るために大義を捨てて、何の武人か」
「Throwing away justice for the sake of his clan, what kind of warrior is that?」

「うむ……」
「Indeed...」

「飽間様は、たとえ一族郎党悉く死に絶える始末となろうが、北朝方へ鞍替えなどなさるまい」
「If it's Akima-sama, even if your entire clan were to go extinct, you would never defect to the North.」

「当然だ」
「Of course.」

「この伊勢國は神宮の膝元。　民が帝を崇め、逆賊を憎む気持ちは、どの國よりも強い」
「This country of Ise is under the protection of the imperial Shinto shrine. The citizens revere the emperor, so their feeling of hatred towards traitors, it is far greater than that of other countries.」
*(Ise --> former province located in the major part of present-day Mie Prefecture and parts of Aichi and Gifu prefectures)

「断じて偽帝に頭は下げられぬ」
「They would never bow their heads to the fake emperor.」

「うむ」
「Indeed.」

「勝たねばならぬ……」
「We must triumph...」

「そのためには、だ。　村正。ぬしの力が要る」
「And, for that. Muramasa. Your power is needed.」

「……」
「……」

「口にはされぬが、帝は待ちかねておられるようだ。　楠木殿もな」
「He does not say it, but the emperor seems to be unable to endure the wait any longer. Kusunoki-dono as well.」

「うむ……」
「Indeed...」

「勢州桑名、千子村の鍛冶長は、五郎正宗の再来ならん……。　その風評が帝のお耳に届き、劒冑鍛造の勅が下って――早三年」
「Seshu Kuwana, Kazuko village's head smith, must return the Gorō Masamune... That rumour reached the emperor's ears, and an imperial decree on Tsurugi forging soon followed. ――3 years has passed since then.」

「まだ出来ぬか」
「Is it still not completed?」

「まだだ」
「Not yet.」

「ぬしの劒冑を楠木殿が身に纏い、南朝全軍を率いて押し出せば、北朝など一夜のうちに滅び去ろう」
「If Kusunoki-dono equips your Tsurugi, and if the whole Southern army were to set out under his command, the North would perish in a single night.」

「大和の民の待ち望む平穏がようやく訪れるであろう……」
「The peace that the people of Yamato have been waiting for would come...」

「うても、そうあらねばならぬと思うておる。　だからこそ、軽々しく鍛造に踏み切れぬ」
「I as well, think that peace must come. However, that is also the exact reason why we must not be rash.」

「やり直しは利かんからの……」
「We only have one chance...」

「まだ工夫がつかぬか」
「Have you not come up with any design?」

「というよりも、方向よな」
「Rather than design, the problem lies in the direction.」

「方向？」
「Direction?」

「飽間様は、至高の劒冑とは如何なるものだと思われる？」
「Akima-sama, what do you think the great Tsurugi is?」

「力が強く、甲鉄は硬く、翼は鋭く速く――」
「It possesses great strength, hard armour, and sharp but swift wings――

「出来るとお思いか？」
「Do you think that's possible?」

「……いや」
「...No.」

「どれほど力量ある鍛冶師でも、万能の劒冑は打てぬ。　何かを選び、何かを捨てねばならぬ」
「No matter how talented the blacksmith, they can't make an all-purpose Tsurugi. Something must be chosen, and something else must be thrown away.」

「その選択が、定まらぬのか」
「So you are unable to settle on a choice?」

「うむ」
「Indeed.」

「何が最善、何が至高か……か？」
「What would be the best, what would be the most... superior?」

「至高の劒冑とはな、飽間様。　役目を遂げる劒冑に他ならぬ」
「Akima-sama, the most superior Tsurugi. It is none other than a Tsurugi that is able to carry out its duty.」

「如何なる者の助けとなり、　如何なる者を討ち滅ぼすのか、　……まずそれを見定めねば、何も始まらぬ」
「To be of help to everyone and everything, or to be the one to bring all to its doom, ...we must first decide on that, or else nothing will start.」

「味方は南朝、敵は北朝であろう？」
「The South is our ally, while the North is our enemy, no?」

「より深く。より細かくだ。　役目が明確であればあるほど、劒冑の性能を特化できる」
「You must think deeper. More precise. As its tasks become clearer, the stronger the Tsurugi becomes.」

「……成程のぅ」
「...I see.」

「機能を定めるにはまず目的を定める必要がある。要はそういうことだ」
「To determine its functions we need to have a clear goal. That's how it is.」

「それで戦場巡りか」
「So that's why you need to go around battlefields?」

「うむ」
「Yes.」

「結論は出せそうか？」
「Have you come with a conclusion then?」

「まだ、掛かるな。　まだ……倒すべき敵の姿が見えぬ」
「Not yet, it's going to take a bit longer. Not yet... I still do not see the form of the enemy that we need to defeat.」

「佐々木如きでは不足だしの」
「Someone like Sasaki is also not enough.」

「そうか……。　わかった。ぬしの存念はそれとなく楠木殿にお伝えしておく」
「I see... Understood. I shall inform Kusunoki-dono of your opinion.」

「帝のお耳にも入ろう。　お二方とも納得される筈だ」
「I will also inform the emperor of this. I should be able to have their consent.」

「済まぬ」
「I'm sorry for the trouble.」

「なに。ぬしとわしの仲だ。　水臭い言葉などいらぬ」
「It's fine. You and I are friends. Do not be reserved.」

「ぬしは心ゆくまで工夫を続けろ。　その間は、わしが賊軍どもから吉野を守り通してみせる」
「Just continue to work to your heart's content. In the mean time, I shall make sure to protect Yoshino from the bandits.

「……頼む」
「...I leave it to you.」

「…………」
「…………」

「どうした、御父。　大層機嫌が悪いようだが」
「What's wrong, Father? You seem to be in a bad mood.」

「…………」
「…………」

「御母？」
「Mother?」

「京の都が奪われたそうです」
「It seems Kyoto has been taken.」

「身を鉄に変え劒冑と成るは蝦夷として生を受けし者の本望、これを厭うなど有り得ぬ事と、説き伏せてはきたが……」

「He was a person who solved the mystery of the universe. In human history, he is the only one who can be called the owner of true wisdom.」

「宇宙の……？　それは以前にお伺いした、あの話のことであろうか」
「The universe...? Are you talking about that topic that I asked about back then?」

「この世には磁気、辰気、創気の三つの源気があるという――」
「There are 3 primordial powers in this world: magnetism, gravity, and chemical bonding――」

「それは、えんぺどくれすの考えを私なりに進めてみたものです。　物理には近付いているはずですが……真理からは離れてしまいました」
「They are ideas of Empedocles which I tried to advance in my own way. I am getting closer to understanding the law of physics... but I have gone further away from the truth.」

「……？」
「……？」

「Emepedocles once said. The world is made out of 4 elements and 2 powers...」

「〝地〟〝陽〟〝海〟〝空〟の四つが〝愛〟の力で結びつき、また〝争い〟の力で別れることによって、世の万象が顕れる。　そう説いたのです」
「"Earth", "Fire", "Water", "Air", these four elements are brought into union by the power of "Love". and are parted from one another by the power of "Strife", thus allowing all things in the world to materialize. That was what he explained.」

「例えば人間は、四種類の元素がほぼ均等に〝愛〟で結ばれることから生まれます。　そして〝愛〟よりも強い〝争い〟の力――怪我や病気――に襲われると死にます」
「For example, human beings are born from the four elements being united with equal powers of "Love". And when "Love" is attacked by "Strife" of a greater power―― such as injuries or death―― we pass away.」

「ふむ……」
「Hmm...」

「この理論で、世のあらゆる物事が説明できます」
「With this theory, it is possible to explain everything in the world.」

「ならば浦夢殿、正義とはいかなるものか？　また、邪悪とは？」
「Then Uramu-dono, what exactly is justice? And what exactly is injustice?」

「Indeed. By all means please teach me.」

「……ありません」
「...There is none.」

「T-That can't be!」

「...True. It is not tangible, but if you consider it as a way of looking at things, then you can say that it exists.」

「見方？」
「Way of looking at things?」

「村正どの。　今、私はここに一つの世界を作りました」
「Muramasa-dono. Right now, I have created a world right here.」

「ふらすこに塩と水を入れてかき混ぜ、蓋をしました。　この閉じた世界には、塩水と空気しかありません」
「I have stirred salt into the water in the flask, and I have covered it. In this closed off world, there is only salt water and air.」

「……」
「……」

「これを、下から火で熱すると」
「If this is heated from below with fire,」

「〝争い〟の力が働きます。　結ばれていた塩と水が別れ、水は水蒸気となって空気と混ざり、塩は結晶に戻ります」
「The power of "Strife" will come into play. The salt and water that were mixed together will seperate, the water will turn into water vapour and be one with the air, and the salt will return to its crystallized form.」

「うむ……」
「I see...」

「さて。　善と悪は、何処にあったでしょうか……」
「Now then. The good and evil, where were they?」

「……」
「……」

「我々の世界に置き換えて、考えてみてください」
「Please think about it in terms of our world.」

「……塩と水を引き離した〝争い〟の力……　火が、悪なのであろうか？」
「...The power of "Strife" that seperated the salt and the water... The fire, would that be the evil?」

「そうですね。　人のつながり、絆は尊いものです。これを引き離すのは罪悪だといえるでしょう……」
「That's true. Relationships between people, bonds are a precious thing. To pull them apart would be a crime...」

「塩と水を塩水にしていた〝愛〟が正義で、引き離した火が邪悪か……」
「So the power of "Love" that combines the salt and water into salt water is justice, and the fire that pulled them apart would be injustice...」

「しかし村正どの。　よく見てください」
「But Muramasa-dono. Please look carefully.」

「塩と水は別れましたが、新たに水と空気が混ざり合い、靄が生まれています」
「Although the salt and water have seperated, the water mixed with the air to produce mist.」

「……むぅ？」
「...Hmm?」

「水と空気の間に〝愛〟が働いたのです。　ということは……火は善でもあったのです」
「The power of "Love" is coming into play between the water and air. This means that... the fire was also good.」

「…………」
「…………」

「今度はこの世界を冷やしてみましょうか」
「This time let us try to cool this world.」

「靄を冷やすと……　水は水滴となって落ちます」
「If the mist is cooled... it will turn back into water and fall as droplets.」

「水滴は塩を溶かし、再び塩水になります」
「The water droplets will dissolve the salt, and then it will once again become salt water.」

「……」
「……」

「塩水を生んだのですから、冷やしたのは善の行いですね。　しかし靄を分解してしまったので、悪でもあります」
「It gave birth to salt water, so the cold is doing a good deed. But since it also seperated the water from the mist, it is evil.」

「ぬ……むぅ」
「Nghh...」

「村正どの。わかりましたか」
「Muramasa-dono. Have you understood?」

「善と悪は――」
「Good and evil――」

「……裏表でしかない、と？」
「...they are two sides of the same coin?」

「そうです。　ある行いを、特定の視点から見た時に善と呼び、逆方向から見た時は悪と呼ぶ」
「Exactly. You may say a certain action is good when you view it from a certain angle, but when viewed from the opposite direction, it is evil.」

「それだけのことに過ぎないのです」
「That is all there is to it.」

「…………」
「…………」

「しかし人々は、この善悪をさも重大なものであるかのように扱っています。　無意識に――あるいは意識的に」
「However, people treat good and evil as if it were something very serious. They do this unconsciously―― and at other times intentionally.」

「何故……？」
「Why...?」

「自分の利益になる〝愛〟を肯定し、自分の損失になる〝争い〟を否定するためです」
「To affirm "Love" that may benefit them, and to deny "Strife" that may cost them.」

「……」
「……」

「この独善こそ、人の心を縛る悪魔の呪い」
「This self-righteousness is the devil's curse that binds the human heart.」

「村正どの……もうおわかりでしょう。　どうして平和は永く続かないのか？　どうして戦争は繰り返されるのか？」
「Muramasa-dono... I'm sure you understand now. Why does peace never last long? Why do wars keep repeating?

「それは――　水は水だけの愛を、空気は空気だけの愛を、塩は塩だけの愛を求めるからです！」
「That's because―― water seeks the love of water alone, air seeks the love of air alone, and salt seeks the love of salt alone!」

「――――」
「――――」

「村正どの……」
「Muramasa-dono...」

「ならば」
「Then」

「世界を正すには」
「to right the world...」

「Please let the people know of the truth that Empedocles found.」

「Release them from the curse! From the curse of fighting against each other due to being trapped in their own personal love.」

「そんな奇跡を成し得るものは……劒冑しかありません。　あなたが、神の劒冑を造るのです！」
「The only thing capable of performing such a miracle is... a Tsurugi. You will make the Tsurugi of god!」

「…………。　できようか……？」

「そして力は、ここに――」
「As for power, it is here――」

「これは？　水晶……いや違う……?」
「What is that? A crystal... No, it's not...?」

「……わ、わからぬ！　馬鹿なっ、蝦夷の知らぬ鉱物など!」
「...I-I do not know! Impossible, for there to be a material unknown to an Emishi!」

「知らないのは当然です。　これはおそらく、地上に一つきりしかないもの……」
「It's only natural for you not to know.  This is probably the only one in the world...」

「聖骸断片。　神の血肉です」
「A fragment from the Holy Sepulchre. This is the flesh and blood of God.

「……神……?　いや、わかる！　確かにこれは――途方もなきものだ!」
「...God...? No, I know!  This is truly―― it is something very valuable!」

「はい。　この石は人を不死にするほどの力を持っています」
「Yes. This stone even has the power to make humans immortal.」

「このように……」

「U-Uramu-dono... that body?!」

「……」

「It is the same... as this stone?

「ええ。　この石を手に入れてから、私は歳を取らず……そして体は次第に、このように変わっていきました」
「Yes. Ever since I've laid my hands on this stone, I have not aged... And then gradually, my body transformed into this.」

「全身が変わる前に、あなたに会えて……　全てを伝えることができて、良かった」
「I'm glad that I got to meet you... and tell you everything before my whole body transformed.」

「私は……　神より授かった使命を、果たせたようです」

「浦夢殿！」

「Not only for one person's love, but the love of all...  Take us―― to the path that pursues universal love, one that does not cause strife, but unites all creations without discrimination!」

「God's―― love...! Please bring it to this world!」

「うむ」

「はい」

「劒冑とは武の器。　戦のためのもの」

「戦とは我の愛を求めて彼の愛を壊す行為。　武とはその暴力」
「War is a conduct carried out for one's own love that in turn destroys other's. War is violence.」

「――――」

「我ら村正は戦を滅ぼす。　戦の悪を人々に知らしめ、戦を人の世から去らしめる！」
「We Muramasas will destroy war. We will make the evil of war be known to the people, and we will drive it off from the human world!」

「武にただ加担するのではなく、　武を制するための劒冑を打つ!」
「We will not make a Tsurugi that can only assist in wars, but rather one that can take control of it!」

「そうだ」

「Hm, what do you mean?  Do you mean you are making two Tsurugis?」

「Of course! Becoming a Tsurugi that is the embodiment of Father's ideals has always been my long-cherished desire.」

「後顧の憂いもない。　こやつには既に、全ての技を伝えてある」
「There is also no need to worry about the future. I have taught this one all of the techniques.」

「……」

「明日より早速、鍛造に掛かろうぞ」
「We will start forging first thing tomorrow.」

「御父の望みが、劒冑をもって人の心中の刃を砕くにあると知ったからには……　その望み、必ずや吾が果たす！」
「Now that I know that Father's desire is to use the Tsurugi to shatter the blade that lies within the people's hearts... I shall fulfill that desire!」

「うむ……！」
「Yes...!」

矢の如く俺の前を過ぎていった光陰は――　ここから急に、精彩を失う。
The memory of that time that passed in front of me like an arrow―― from here on out, it suddenly lost its colour.

三世村正は、これ以降の事変の殆どを自分の眼では見なかったのだろう。　幾つかの短い映像と伝聞で得たらしき情報とがひとまとめに、俺の認識上を滑ってゆく。
Third-generation Muramasa must not have seen most of the disaster that followed thereafter with her own eyes. Several short images and information that seemed like it was obtained from hearsay slipped through my mind all at once. 

遂に完成した始祖村正そして二世村正、この二領の劒冑は性能において頂点へ達していたのは無論だが、加えて異常な特質を備えてもいた。　それは千子村正だけのものであり、二つあった。
Founder Muramasa and second-generation Muramasa have finally done it, these two Tsurugis naturally stand at the top in terms of their abilities , but at the same time, they also possessed certain abnormal characteristics.

一つは〝善悪相殺〟の戒律である。　対敵を一人殺したなら味方も一人。悪しき者を一人殺したなら善き者も一人。憎む者を一人殺したなら、愛する者もまた一人、殺さねばならない。
One of which is the precept of "counterbalancing good and evil". If you kill a foe, you must kill an ally. If you kill an evil person, you must kill a good person. If you kill a person filled with hatred, then you must too, kill a person filled with love.

村正と結縁した武者はこの掟を背負う。　己の善のみ盲信し、敵の善は悪と看做して排除する、その〝独善〟を力で押し通すことを、村正という劒冑は許さないのだ。
Mushas who form a link with Muramasa must bear the burden of this law. To blindly believe in one's own goodness, and disregard the good of the enemy in the process, to use that "self-righteousness" as power to have one's own way, the Tsurugi known as Muramasa will not allow that.

衆に卓抜する村正の暴威で望みを遂げようとすれば、己の手でその望みを打ち砕く結末に至る。　村正武者は最強にして、誰よりも武力の行使を自重する人物にならざるを得ないであろう。
Should one try to fulfill one's own desires using Muramasa's superior might, they will end up destroying that very desire with their own hands. While the musha who uses Muramasa does need to be the strongest of them all, they must also be someone who is able to show the most restraint when it comes to the usage of violence.

もう一つは〝精神同調〟の能である。　村正は『波』を放散し、周囲の人間の精神に仕手のそれを重ねることができるのだ。
The other characteristic is the ability of "spirit alignment". Muramasa will radiate "waves", and with that it will be able to impose its spirit on the people in the surrounding area.

仕手の精神に浸透した善悪相殺の戒律も写される。　一軍全体を、村正の思想に沿う集団へと変貌せしめられるのである。
Those whose spirits have been imposed upon will have the precept of counterbalancing good and evil thrust upon them. With that, it is possible to transform an entire army into a group that is in line with Muramasa's ideals.

武者ならば甲鉄の防護力をもって『波』の力に抵抗するも可能だが……　村正はこの能力の変形として『卵』を生成する事で、遂には武者の精神をも逃さぬのだった。
Mushas may possibly be able to resist the power of the "waves" by using iron armours, however... Muramasa can produce "eggs" as a variant of this ability, and with this, the spirits of the warriors will no longer be able to get away.

『卵』は劒冑に移植されると内部で生育、やがて孵化し、劒冑を『波』の中継点に造り替える。　新たに発散される『波』の影響を第一に受けるのは、最も近くにいる者、つまりその劒冑の仕手である……。
The "eggs" that are planted by the Tsurugi will grow inside the person's body, eventually it will hatch, and then it will become a relay point that can also produce the "waves". The first ones who will be affected by the newly emitted "waves" are those that are the closest in proximity, in short, they are under the Tsurugi's 

村正の仕手に利己心あらば、この〝精神同調〟能力を味方の軍に対して使おうとは思わないであろう。　敵軍に対して用い、戦意を奪おうとする筈である。
If those under Muramasa's influence had a selfish nature, they would definitely not want to use the power of "spirit alignment" on their allies. They would want to use it against the enemy army to take away their will to fight.

しかし、だからこそ始祖村正は劒冑を二領用意して、対立する両陣営に与えたのだ。　双方の村正武者が敵に対して〝精神同調〟を行使し合えば、一方だけが優勢になるような事態は起きない。
However, that is exactly why Founder Muramasa had prepared two Tsurugis and gave them to both factions. If both mushas of Muramasa were to use the "spirit alignment" on each other, there would be no way for only one side to gain the upper hand.

戦場は遍く〝善悪相殺〟の戒律に支配される。
The whole battlefield will then be directed by the precept of "counterbalancing good and evil".

完璧――そう言って良かった。　始祖村正が劒冑に懸けた理想は、これ以上はないという形で結実した。
It can be said that it was perfect. The ideals that Founder Muramasa had put into the Tsurugi came into fruition in a way that cannot be surpassed.

この劒冑は必ずや世に平和をもたらす。　長きに渡り続いた南北朝の乱を、穏健に終息させる。
This Tsurugi will definitely bring peace into the world. It will bring a peaceful end to the long war between the Northern and Southern courts.

始祖村正はそう信じた。　二世村正も信じ、三世村正も疑わなかった。
Founder Muramasa believed as much. Second-generation Muramasa also believed, and the third-generation Muramasa also did not doubt it.

…………が。　　事実はそうならなかったことを、後世に生きる俺は知っている。
...However, as someone who lived in the future, I know that things did not turn out that way.

南北朝の時代は――　その最後に未曾有の殲滅戦争を巻き起こし、わずか一年で当時の全人口の一割とも二割以上とも云われる死者を出して、閉幕へ至るのだ。
The era of the Northern and Southern dynasties―― An unprecendented war of annilihation happened near the end of that era, bringing it to a close after killing an estimate of more than 10 to 20 percent of the population of the time within just a year.  

災厄の劒冑。　三代で絶えた妖甲の一門、千子右衛門尉村正の銘を歴史に刻んで。
A Tsurugi of calamity. The name Sengou Uemon-no-jou Muramasa, a family of three generations that brought forth the Tsurugi of calamity , was carved into history.

そこは雅やかで、されど落ち着いた佇まいだった。　何処かの御殿の、内庭……そんな風情だ。
An elegant place with a calm atmosphere. It seems to be the inner garden... of some palace.

その場で、俺――村正は平伏している。　前方の段階には誰かが立ち、こちらを見下ろしている様子であった。
In that place, I―― Muramasa, was on my knees. Someone was standing on the stairs in front of me, seemingly looking down on me. 

人は、それきり。　辺りに気配はあるが、遠ざけられているようだ。
That's how much people amounted to. You can sense their presence around you, but it seems they always keep themselves at a distance.

「そなたが村正の孫……三代目か」
「So you are the third generation... the grandchild of Muramasa.」

「は……っ、はい。　へ、陛下に置かれましては――」
「Y-Yes... It is a great honour to be in Your Majesty's presence――」

「良い。今は公衆の前でも朝議の場でもない。　慣れぬ言葉遣いは無用にいたせ」
「Don't mind it. We are not in the council chamber, and the public is not here to see us. There is no need for such formalities.」

「は、はい……」
「Y-Yes...」

……陛下。　では、この御方は帝か。おそらく南朝の。
...Your Majesty. Then that person must be the emperor. Most likely the South's.

「既に聞いておろうが……」
「You should've heard already, but...」

「……」
「……」

「村正、そなたの家門は――これを断絶する。　一切の継承は許さぬ」
「Muramasa, your lineage is hereby severed. You will not be allowed any inheritance.」

「劒冑鍛冶右衛門尉村正は、そなたをもって終えよ」
「Tsurugi blacksmith Uemon-no-jou Muramasa, its lineage will end with you.」

「…………。　承知して、おります」
「...I understand.」

「我が一門の犯したる罪……招きたる災いの程を思えば……　祖先に遡り、一族係累鏖殺の憂目に遭おうとも恨み言は申せませぬところ」
「When I think of the sin that my clan has commited... one that brought such calamity upon us... even if all of my family members and my ancestors were massacred, I will bear no grudge.」

「陛下の御慈悲に……感謝いたします……」
「I am truly grateful... for Your Majesty's mercy...」

「……うむ……」
「...Yes...」

家門断絶。　中世の価値観においてその一事がどれほどの重みを持つのか。現代人には知る由もないことだ。
The severance of a clan. The people of today have no way of knowing how much weight such an event would have to those living in the Middle Ages.

ただ、村正の両手の震えと……　白砂の上へしたたり落ちる雫から、推し量るしかなかった。
However, from Muramasa's trembling hands... and the droplets that fell unto the white sand, I can only guess.

全ては罪のため。招いた災いのため。
Everything was to right that sin. For the calamity that was brought forth. --> hmm maybe 

俺は知った。　南北朝時代最後の惨劇――そこに秘められた真実を。
I knew. The last tragedy that happened during the Nanboku-chō period―― and the truth behind it.

――――たった一つの事故が何もかも狂わせた。
A single incident has put everything out of order.

始祖村正を贈られた北朝軍の主将は、当時、堅牢な権力基盤を有しているとは言い難い状況にあった。　支配者というよりも、諸将の利害調整役という立場に近かった。
The general of the North who was bestowed with the Founder Muramasa was in a situation where he could not be said to have a solid power base. Rather than a ruler, he was closer to a coordinator of interests among the generals.

政治の才に優れた実弟の力を借りて、漸う軍をまとめていたのである。　些細な情勢の変化、利害関係の変動から敵意を買い、昨日までの部下に盾突かれることも一切ではなかった。
With the help of his younger brother who had an aptitude for politics, he was finally able to organize an army. He took advantage of the slight changes in the current state of affairs, bought off his enemies according to the change in interests, and all that without causing a rebellion from his subordinates.

それは彼が村正を手に入れてまだ程ない頃のことである。　出陣前の慌しさに紛れて刺客が主将の側まで近付き、不意に襲い掛かった。
It was not long after he had his hands on Muramasa. In the hustle and bustle before going into battle, an assassin approached the general and unexpectedly attacked him.

戦慣れした主将は反射的に抜刀し、刺客を斬り――　殺してしまったのだ。
The battle hardened general reflexively drew his sword and slashed the assasin―― thus killing him.

村正の戒律が持つ拘束力は絶対である。　敵を殺した彼は自分の意思によらずして刃の向きを返し、傍らに立つ味方を斬り伏せた。
The binding force of Muramasa's precept was absolute. Having killed his enemy, he unwillingly turned his blade towards his ally who stood beside him, and took his life.

公私両面で彼を支えてくれていた、最愛の弟を。
It was his beloved brother who had supported him in both his official and personal affairs. 

……その日から、北朝軍は狂気の集団と化した。　発狂した主将が〝精神同調〟の波を無差別に放散し、全軍に己が狂気を蔓延させたのである。
...Ever since that day, the Northern army turned into a group filled with madness. The mad general radiated the waves of "spirit alignment" without discrimination, and thus spreading his madness throughout the whole army.

狂将率いる狂兵の群れを迎えて――　二世村正を持つ南朝方の主将は、狂気の『波』から味方を守るため、先んじて全軍を自分の精神影響下へ置くよりほかに手立てがなくなった。
In the face of an army spearheaded by a mad general―― the commander of the Southern army who had the second-generation Muramasa, in order to protect his allies from the "waves" of madness, had no choice but to preemptively place the entire army under his mental influence.

かくして前例のない地獄的な闘争が地上に発現する。
Thus, an unprecedented hellish struggle emerged on earth.

一方は、手当たり次第何もかも破壊し殺し尽くさんとする魔獣の群れ。　一方は、敵兵を一人殺す都度、肩並べて戦う友をも一人ずつ殺してゆく悲愴の軍団。
On one side was a pack of beasts who indescriminately destroys and kills everything until nothing was left. On the other side was a pitiful army that kills its own allies for every enemy that they kill.

末世の相そのものであった。　この世において人間の生命は秋の田の稲穂のように、無造作に刈り取られ、三途の川の向こうへ流された。
It was truly the Latter Days of the Dharma itself. In this world, human life is like the ears of rice in the autumn fields, easily harvested and swept away to the other side of the Sanzu River.
(TL/N: Latter Days of the Dharma --> 2000 years after the passing of Buddha. An age where the teaching of Buddhism are lost, and the world if filled with conflict.)

どれほどの人が死に、どれほどの村が滅んだか……　正確に知る者など誰もいない。知ろうとする意欲を持つ者もいなかったろう。
No one knew exactly how many people have died, or how many villages have been destroyed... No one had the desire to find out. 

乱の最中、人々はただ生き延びるために必死であり、乱が果てた後は、世間の惨状にただ呆然とするばかりであった。
In the middle of war, people were just desperately trying to survive, and once the war was over, they will be stunned by the disastrous scene before them. 

神懸かりの力を揮った始祖村正と北朝主将に南朝の将とその麾下十三騎が挑み、遂にこれを討ち果たして乱の源を断った時――曰く「いまや大和では人よりも、死肉を食らう犬猫の方が栄えている」……。
The commander of the South and his 13 cavalrymen faced off against the Northern general and the Founder Muramasa who wielded divine power. When the source of the war has finally been cut off by the North's defeat―― it was said 
"in Japan of that time, dogs and cats that feast on dead flesh were more prosperous than people"...

ある法師の嘆弁である。
The lament of Buddhist priest.

「村正よ……」
「Muramasa...」

「……」
「……」

「そなたら一門に悪心がなかったことは良くわかっている。　乱世を収めたかったのであろう……」
「We are well aware that you and your clan did not have any evil intentions. You all must have wanted to bring a close to these turbulent times...」

「元を糺せば、民の苦難も顧みず戦を続けた朕の罪こそ重い……。　もそっと早く、北朝と和しておれば、このような仕儀とはならなんだ」
「In actuality, it is Our sin that is heavy, We had continued the war without regard for the suffering of Our people... If We had made peace with the North ealier, things would not have come to such an outcome.」

「…………」
「…………」

「いずれ朕の罪は天の罰するところとなろう」
「Sooner or later We will be punished by the heavens for Our sins.」

「が……それでも村正よ、朕は社稷を預かる者として、国土に災禍をもたらしたそなたらを許すわけにはゆかぬ。　わけてもそなたの祖父と母は……」
「But even so... Muramasa, as someone who is in charge of this nation, We cannot forgive you for the calamity that you have brought upon the land. Especially your grandfather and mother...」

「始祖村正は粉々に砕かれ、既に跡形もない。　楠木の二世村正は深く傷ついたが……まだ滅びておらぬ……」
「Founder Muramasa have been broken into many pieces, and no trace was left. Kusunoki's second-generation Muramasa was critically damaged... but it is not yet destroyed...」

「これを……このままにはしておけぬ」
「Things... cannot be left this way.」

「……！」
「……！」

「近いうちに砕き、鋳潰す……。　さよう心得よ」
「In the near future, it will be destroyed and melted down... Be aware of this.」

「……お、お待ちを……　陛下！」
「...P-Please wait... Your Majesty!」

「……」
「……」

「どうか……その儀ばかりは！」
「Please... anything but that!」

「二世村正を潰すなと云うか」
「Are you telling me not to destroy second-generation Muramasa?」

「蝦夷にとり、劒冑となるは本望。　戦場にて斃され、土に朽ちるもまた本望」
「As an Emishi, becoming a Tsurugi is our long cherished ambition. To fall on the battlefield, to decay and return to earth, it is also our long cherished ambition.」

「さ、されど……　ひとたび劒冑となりながら、戦なき場所で鉄屑に戻され棄てられるは――蝦夷として、鍛冶師として、死にも堕獄にも勝る痛哭！」
「B-Be that as it may... once we have become a Tsurugi, for us to be thrown away and turned into scraps of iron in a place other than a battlefield―― as an Emishi, as a blacksmith, that is a pain even worse than death or falling into hell!」

「……そうか。　そうであったのう……」
「...I see. I see...」

「だが戦で葬るには、今一度、あの恐ろしき劒冑を誰かに装甲させねばならぬ……。　さようなことを、朕が許せると思うてか」
「But for it to be buried in the battle, someone must once again, equip that terryfying Tsurugi... Did you think We will let that happen?」

「…………」
「…………」

「武の器は戦場にて朽ちねばならぬもの……　それが叶わぬならいっそ封印され、永劫の眠りにつき、忘れ去られるを望むものにございます」
「A warrior's vessel are meant to decay on the battlefield... If that is not possible, I wish it could be sealed into eternal sleep instead, and be forgotten forever.」

「どうか、陛下……！　この首を献じて、お願い申し上げます」
「Please, Your Majesty...! I make this plea with my head as an offer」

「……」
「……」

「先ほど、陛下はお認め下さいました……。　祖父と母に悪心は無かったと。乱世に幕を引きたかっただけなのだと」
「Your Majesty has deemed so ealier... that grandfather and mother had no evil intentions, that they only wanted to bring an end to these turbulent times. 」

「その通りなのです！　我が祖が、何を誤っていたとしても、その願いだけは……正しかった筈なのです……！」
「You were absolutely right! No matter what mistakes they have commited, their hearts... were in the right place...!」

「二世が劒冑として最も卑しき最期を遂げれば……その理念までも汚されてしまいます！」
「If mother were to meet a worse end... then even their principles will be tainted!」

「…………」
「…………」

「土に埋めて頂いても構いません。　海に沈めて頂いても構いません」
「It's fine if you bury it in the ground. It's fine if you sank it into the sea.」

「ですがどうか、鋳潰しだけはお許しを……」
「But please, anything except for melting it down...」

「……」
「……」

「土に埋めても、掘り返されるやもしれぬ。　海に沈めても、引き上げられるやもしれぬ」
「Even if it is buried in the ground, there is a chance it could be dug up. Even if it is sank into the sea, there is a chance that it can be pulled up.」

「そうして、村正の劒冑が大和に還り……　再び、地上を地獄に変えるやもしれぬ」
「Then, the Tsurugi of Muramasa will come back to the lands of Japan... and once more, this earth will be turned into living hell.」

「……っ」
「...」

「村正よ。　首を献ずるとの言葉に、嘘はあるまいな」
「Muramasa. I hope you're not lying when you say you'll give up your head.」

「は――はい！」
「Y-Yes!」

「御寛恕を賜れるのであれば、いつなりと」
「If you are willing to extend your generosity, I shall gladly do so.」

「宜しい。　ならば三世村正、そなたに命ずる」
「Very well. Then, third-generation Muramasa, We hereby command you」

「劒冑を打て」
「Forge a Tsurugi.」

「……?」
「……?」

「そなたの母に比肩する劒冑となるのだ」
「Become a Tsurugi that is able to rival your mother.」

「そして、母と共にいずこかの山陰で眠れ。　願わくば永劫」
「And sleep with your mother in a place in the shade of a mountain somewhere.　Hopefully for eternity.」

「だが……そなたを共に封ずる理由は、ほかでもない。　わかるであろうな」
「However... the reason you will be sealed together, there is none other. You are aware, are you not?」

「……」
「……」

「将来、何者かが封印を破り、二世村正を手にした時。　そなたもまた、仕手を求めよ」
「In the future, if someone broke the seal, and laid their hands on second-generation Muramasa. You too must find a master」

「そして母を監視するのだ。　そなたの祖父が願った通り、世に和を導く力として用いられるなら良い。だがもし当世と同様、災いの武者となり果てし時は――」
「and keep an eye on your mother. If they are able to become a force that guides this world into peace, then that is excellent. But if they became a musha that brings calamity similar to the present-day, then――」

「そなたが二世村正を討たねばならぬ」
「you must defeat second-generation Muramasa.」

「…………」
「…………」

「それができぬと申すなら、やはり二世村正は潰すほかにない」
「If you say you are unable to do so, then there is no other option but to destroy second-generation Muramasa.」

「答えよ、三世。　そなたは母を討つことができるか……？」
「Answer, third-generation. Are you able to defeat your mother...?」

「で――できます！　必ずや、御諚の通りにいたします！」
「I-I can! I will definitely do as you command!」

「良かろう」
「Very well.」

「ならば、繰り返し言い置くぞ。　劒冑となったそなたが武人と結縁するは、母が解き放たれた時のみ」
「Then We will say it once more. You who have become a Tsurugi will form a connection with a warrior, only if your mother has been released.」

「その時が訪れるまでは、何者とも帯刀の儀を執り行ってはならぬ」
「Until that time comes, no one is to perform the ceremony to equip a Tsurugi.」

「はい」
「Yes.」

「今ひとつ。　祖父の秘法をもって劒冑となれば、そなたもあの忌むべき能を備えるのであろう」
「One more thing. If you are to become a Tsurugi with your grandfather's secret technique, you may possess that detestable ability.」

「人の心を侵す〝波〟を操るのであろう」
「The ability to produce "waves" that invades the hearts of people.」

「……はっ……」
「...Yes...」

「朕はあれこそが、そなたの祖父の、唯一の過ちであったと……そう思えてならぬ」
「We can't help but think that... that one thing, was your grandfather's sole mistake.」

「そなたの祖父は急ぎ過ぎたのだ。　願いは正しくとも……人心を強引に従えるやりようは、余りに性急であった」
「Your grandfather was too hasty. Though his heart was in the right place... the way he forcibly subdued people's hearts, it was impetuous.」

「ゆえに……ああなった……」
「Because of that... things turned out that way...」

「…………」
「…………」

「村正よ。命じておく。〝波〟の使用は、朕の名をもって禁ずる」
「Muramasa. We command you. By Our name, the use of the "waves" are hereby forbidden.」

「如何なる理由があろうとも、この禁を破りし時は、そなたはもはや朕の臣ではない。　朝敵、逆賊である」
「No matter the reason, should you break this prohibition, you will no longer be Our subject. You will be deemed a traitor, an enemy to the crown.」

「……!」
「……!」

「良いな。　この儀、しかと命じたぞ！」
「Understood? We have certainly gave out the command!」

「はっ……！」
「Yes...!」

「……うむ……」
「...Very well...」

「祈っておるぞ、千子右衛門尉村正。　そなたと母が、二度と目覚めぬよう……」
「We pray, Sengou Uemon-no-jou Muramasa. That you and your mother, will never wake up...」

「長き刻の果て、解き放たれることがあっても……その時こそは、そなたの祖父の願いを叶えるために使われるよう」
「That at the ends of time, even if you are released...  at that time, you can finally fulfill your grandfather's wish.」

「そなたと母が相争うことなどなきよう……　天地神明に祈っておく」
「We pray to the gods of heaven and earth... that you will not have to fight your mother.」

「…………」
「…………」

……そうして、村正の過去は終わる。
...And so, Muramasa's past came to an end.

村正は劒冑と成り――　母と共に、一人の武士に託され、山奥の地にて封じられる。
Muramasa was to become a Tsurugi―― Alongside her mother, they were entrusted to a warrior, and sealed away somewhere deep within the mountain.

白銀の女王蟻と深紅の蜘蛛。　二領の劒冑は長い長い刻を、眠りの裡に過ごした。
A silver queen ant and a crimson spider. The two Tsurugis spent a long, long time in deep slumber.

――――――――あの日まで。
―――――――― Until that day.

おかしな話かもしれないが、市内の署長宅で過ごすより拘置所の一室にいる方が俺は落ち着く。
It may sound strange, but I feel more at ease spending my days in the prison rather than at the chief's house in the city.

殺人犯が一般市民の中に紛れているという状況にはやはり違和感を拭い去れないからだ。　罪人は隔離されていてこそ自然である。
It's because I can't shake the feeling of discomfort that a murderer is living in the midst of the general public.　It is only natural that criminals should be isolated.

大鳥主従が公用で暫く署長宅を空けるとの事だったので、この機に俺も牢獄へ戻る事にした。　一条には、少し留守にするとだけ伝えてある。
Since Chief Otori was going to leave the house for some time due to an official business, I decided to take this opportunity to return to the prison.　I only told Ichijou that I will be away for a while. 

銀星号の痕跡が見つかり次第また市中に戻らねばならないが、それまでは囚人の日々を過ごせるだろう。　心に波風立たぬ時間を得られるという事だ。
We will have to return to the city as soon as any traces of the Silver Star is found, but we should be able to spend our days as a prisoner until that time comes. Which means I will have time to clear my mind.

そしてそれは無論、惰眠を貪るために求めたものではない。
And of course, I'm not doing this because I wanted to laze about. 

――如何にして墜とすべきか。
―― How can we defeat it? 

銀星号は人の世に災いなす魔王。　暴勇にして狂気の武者、しかも狂気を唄い衆に広め無益な惨死へ駆り立ててゆく。
The Silver Star is a demon king that brings calamity to the human world. He is a musha filled with madness despite his bravery, and worse yet he spreads madness to the people that drives them to a futile and miserable death.

決して、俺の手で倒さねばならぬ。　……二年前、何の不幸でそうなってしまったにせよ、もはや光を正気に戻せるとは思えなかった。試す時間もない。あれは呼吸するように人命を散らすのだから。
I must defeat him with my own hands... I don't know what kind of misfortune happened two years ago that made him that way, but I could no longer believe that it is possible to bring Hikaru back to his senses. There is also no time to try. It scatters human lives like its breathing. 

倒さねばならない、が――問題はその現実的手法。　天地隔絶の戦力差を、如何様にして覆したものか。
It must be defeated, but―― the problem is how. How would it be possible, to overcome a difference in strength that is like heaven and earth. 

武界の通論に云う。　武者の戦力は仕手の技量、劒冑の性能、両者の連携、この三項の総合で決する――と。
A common theory in the world of martial arts. A musha's strength is determined by three factors: the skills of the wielder, the abilities of the Tsurugi, and the coordination between the two. 

第一。俺と光の技量差は動かし難い。　天性の才能の差なのだ。諦めるつもりも鍛錬を怠るつもりもないが、一朝一夕に埋められる質の差でないという事実は正しく認めておく必要があるだろう。
First. The difference in skill between Hikaru and I is undeniable. It's a difference in natural talent. I have no intention on giving up or neglecting my training, but it may be necessary to acknowledge the fact that it is not a gap that can be overcome in a single night.

第二。劒冑の性能に大きな差はない。　これは俺の実感である。二世村正の引辰制御は脅威と呼ぶほかない能力だが、三世村正の磁流制御もそれに匹敵し得るだけのものだ。
Second. The gap between the Tsurugis is not that large. I have personally experienced this. The second Muramasa's ability to control gravity is a threatening ability, but it is something that the third Muramasa's ability of controlling magnetic currents can rival.

第三。
Third.

「…………」
「…………」

仕手と劒冑の連携。
Coordination between the Tsurugi and its wielder.

ここ最近、あの老人の言葉を頻繁に思い起こすのは、無意識の部分がその事実を示唆しようとしていたからなのか……。
I've been thinking about that old man's words frequently these days, and I wonder if it's because some unconscious part of me has been trying to suggest that fact.

「しかし、それだけ装甲を重ねているにしては……御堂、なれはあまり劔冑のことを信頼しておらぬようだな？」
「But despite having so many armours... Midou, you don't seem to have faith in Tsurugis, do you?」

「昨日からなれとあの赤い劔冑を見ておると、どうも……な。　どこか、うまく噛み合っておらぬ気がするのだ」
「I've been looking at that red Tsurugi with you since yesterday, and well... I feel like you both don't mesh well in some way.」

「劔冑は道具……それは、事実。　しかし魂を持つ道具であることを忘れてはならんのではないか？」
「Tsurugis are tools... that is a fact. But we shouldn't forget that they are tools with a soul, no?」

（弥源太老）
（Old Yagenta)

あの時は、貴重な忠告を突っ撥ねたのだった。　心が有ろうが無かろうが道具は道具、使い手の意思のみで――全てを使い手の責任において扱いきるべきものだ、と。
At that time, I brushed off his valuable advice. I told him that whether or not it has a heart, a tool is a tool, it is only a reflection of its user's will―― Its use should completely be the responsibility of its master.

今とてその存念が何か変化したわけではない。　劒冑を使う責任、使った結果に対する責任は仕手が一人で担うもので、誰とも分かち合えないし、分かち合ってはならない。そう思う。
It's not that I have changed my mind. The responsibility of using a Tsurugi, and the responsibility in regards to the results that came for using it should be shouldered by its user alone, it is not something that can or should be shared with anyone else.

だが……
However...

（俺は村正の事をまるで知らなかった）
（I didn't know anything about Muramasa.)

善悪相殺。　あの奇妙な戒律の意味。
Counterbalancing good and evil. The meaning of that odd precept.

知らなかったのは、村正が語ろうとしなかったからでもある。　しかし、俺の側で積極的に知ろうとする意思を持たなかった事も理由である。
The reason I didn't know anything was because Muramasa did not talk about it. However, it was also because I didn't have the will to actively find out.

ただ、呪わしい劒冑なのだと思っていた。　そう決めつけ、忌むことで――
I just thought that it was an accursed Tsurugi. I arbitrarily decided so, and abhorred it――

俺の罪も、光の罪も……　何もかも、この妖甲に祟られた所為なのだと。
My sins, and that of Hikaru... everything, they were all the results of being haunted by this demon armor, was what I thought.

だが青江貞次との戦闘が、秘められた真実を教えてくれた。　村正の戒律は、世と人への悪意から付加されたものではない――
But the battle with Sadaji Aoe taught me a hidden truth.　Muramasa's precepts were not added out of malice for the world and people――

むしろ乱世を正さんとする思いからだった。　それが、完全に裏目に出……南北朝の時代をこの上なく凄惨な形で閉じさせる事になった。
Rather, it was out of a desire to correct the turbulent times. But it completely backfired... and the era of the Northern and Southern courts ended in the most horrific way possible.

あの災厄の再現が今、銀星号によって為されている。　　　だから、なのだ。
The calamity is now being reenacted by the Silver Star. That is why.

（……村正）
（...Muramasa)

だから村正は劒冑の身でありながら、仕手に責任を委ねず、自分の責任において戦おうとしていたのだ。　一族の罪を、自分の手で贖おうと。
That is why despite being a Tsurugi, Muramasa did not leave the responsibility to her wielder, but is trying to fight on her own responsibility. She wanted to atone for the sins that her clan commited with her own hands.

そうして俺達は互いに背を向け合った。　互いを見ないままに、突き詰めれば自分の意思と力のみで戦おうとしていた。
And so we both turned our backs on each other. Without caring for each other, we wanted to fight with our own power. 

……銀星号に勝てる道理がない。
...There was no way we could've won against the Silver Star.

責任意識のためであろうと、心の逃げ場を作るためであろうと、互いに認め合わない仕手と劒冑が武者としてまともに働けるかと問えば、答えは否だ。　何故なら両者の関係はまず相互承認から始まる。
Whether it is because of a sense of responsibility or to create a place for one's heart to take refuge, when it comes to the question of whether or not a Tsurugi and its wielder who don't approve of each other could work together, the answer would be "no". That's because everything could only begin when the both of them have acknowledged each other. 

互いに資質を問い、認め合う事で、縁が結ばれ武者となる。　これを古来、帯刀の儀と云う。
By getting to know each other's nature and recognizing each other, a bond will be formed, and one will become a musha. Since ancient times, this has been said to be the ceremony of equipping a tsurugi.

Two years ago, Muramasa and I had only done an informal ceremony due to very urgent circumstances. We never did a formal ceremony after that. I didn't wish to do it, and Muramasa didn't show any signs of wanting to do so either.

つまり俺と村正は、実は武者として話にならぬ欠陥の持ち主なのだ。　それをこれまでは、問題にもならぬ事、鍛錬で補いがつく程度の事だと思い捨ててきた。

Spirit contamination.

That's right. In that dream of the past, the power of spirit contamination was strictly forbidden with an imperial order. The importance that people from the middle ages places on the imperial family can't be compared to people of today. That order was absolute... or at least it was supposed to be.

果たして村正は――少なくとも表面上――何ら動揺を示さなかった。
But sure enough, Muramasa―― at least on the surface―― did not show any signs being shaken.

《...The only thing that hasn't faded since that time is my armor and my mission. It's a simple feat to crush your will that has gotten in the way.》

〝従いなさい〟

我がものならぬ思念が、心中に芽生える。　これは……村正の？
A thought that shouldn't belong to me sprouts in my mind. This is... Muramasa's?

精神汚染とはこういうものか。　これは――まずい。抗う術がない。
So this is spirit contamination. This is―― bad. I don't have the means to go against it.

〝従いなさい〟

Leaving out all reason, I came to that conclusion. I can't be away from Muramasa, not now. At any rate I need to go after her!

追わねば、俺はきっと生涯悔いる。
I need to go after her, or else I will regret it for the rest of my life.

だが……　どうしたものか。

拘置囚の身に自由はない。　署長に連絡し、釈放の手続きを踏んで貰うにも時間が掛かる。
There are no freedom for prisoners.  Contacting the chief to take care of the release procedures will also take up time.

最短でも数時間必要だ。　…………間に合うか?
It will take a few hours at the very least... will I make it in time? 

屋根から屋根。　梢から梢へと跳ね渡る。
From roof to roof. Jumping across treetop to treetop.

当ては何もない。　ただ、立ち止まっていたくなかった。
I had no aim. I just didn't want to stop.

日没にはまだ間のある時間帯だ。こんな乱雑な移動をしていては人目につくだろう。　　しかし――どうでもいい。
There is still some time before sunset. People would probably notice since I'm moving in such a chaotic manner. But―― I don't care anymore.

今はこのまま馳せ回り、身にまといつく何かを振り払いたい。　……その何かは外皮ではなく内面に張り付いたもので、いくら駆けようが剥がれはしないと悟っていたが。
Right now I'd like to keep running around like this, and shake off whatever it is that's clinging on to me. Even though I do understand that no matter how much I ran it won't peel off, since it's something that is clinging on to me on the inside, and not outside.

（認められる――わけが、ない）

俺の意思を認めてくれ、と。　自分の意思で戦い、責任を負うことを認めて欲しいと……それだけを望んだ仕手に、完全な拒絶を返した。
Please acknowledge my wish. I want you to acknowledge the fact that I'm fighting out of my own will, and that I also bear responsibility for it, he said... I completely rejected a user who only asked for that much.

彼は私の意志を認めると言ってくれたのに。　あの錆びた錠前のような頑固者が。なのに。　　けれどどうしても、それは認められないのだ。
Even though he acknowledged my wish. That person who was as stubborn as a rusty lock. And yet. Even then, I couldn't acknowledge it.

青江との交戦中、彼が私の過去を見たように、私も昔日の彼を見ていた。　だから知っている。
During the battle with Aoe, just as he saw my past, I also saw his. That's why I know.

彼は本来、小さな町で穏やかに暮らす人間であったことを。　その生活を奪ったのが、私と先代――二領の村正だということを。
He was originally a man who lived peacefully in a small town. And the one who robbed him of that livelihood, was me and my predecessor―― the second-generation Muramasa.

村正の存在さえなかったなら、彼は平穏な日々を命尽きるまで続けられたのだ。　……五百年前、私が愚かなことを願わなければ！
If the Muramasas didn't exist, he would have been able to continue living in peace until his life is exhausted... If only I didn't ask for such a foolish thing 500 years ago!

（母様を、見捨てるべきだった。　見捨てなくてはいけなかった）

帝の御意に服し、破壊させておけば良かったのだ。　それがどれほど屈辱的で、無念で、蝦夷の劒冑鍛冶として受け入れ難い仕儀であろうとも。
I should have obeyed the emperor's will and let her be destroyed. No matter how humiliating it would have been, no matter how mortifying, no matter how hard it would be to accept as a tsurugi blacksmith of the Emishi, I should have done so.

肉親の情など、川に流して。　鍛冶師の矜持など、犬に食わせて。　　何となればこの手で、二世を潰すべきだったのだ！
Things such as familial love, I should have let it be washed away by the river. I should have fed this pride of a blacksmith to the dogs. If anything, I should have destroyed the second with my own hands!

（それができなかったばかりに！）
（Just because I couldn't do that!)

〝銀星号〟は出現した。　南北朝の昔の悪夢が、この興隆という時代において黄泉帰ってしまった。
The "Silver Star" appeared. The nightmare from back during the Nanboku-chō period has turned this age of prosperity into hell.

これは、私の決断一つで防げたことなのだ。　生前の私の柔弱な心が、この災いを――無数の死を招いた。
This is something that could have been prevented with my one decision. The weakness in my heart, I caused this disaster―― I caused countless death.

銀星号との戦いはつまり、私の過ちに対する決着にほかならない。　それを己のものとして背負うと言う景明の意思など、どうして認められよう。
In other words, the fight with the Silver Star is none other than a way to settle my mistake. How could I accept Kageaki's wish to also bear this burden?

妖甲千子村正一門の愚行に巻き込まれただけの彼が、苛酷な闘争に苦しみ魂までも傷つくことを、どうして！
For what reason would he, who was dragged into this, and even got his soul wounded because of the harsh struggle, do that?! 

（認められるわけないじゃない……）
（How could I acknowledge it...)

私の犯した過ちはほかにもある。
I've also commited other mistakes.

善悪相殺。あの戒律。　あの呪い――
Counterbalancing good and evil. That precept. That curse――

せめてあれさえなかったなら、景明の手で殺させる人間の数は半分で済んだ。　苦しみもいくらか和らいだろう。
If only that didn't exist, the number of people who had to be killed by Kageaki's hands would have been halved. He wouldn't have had to suffer as much.

自分は始祖や二世とは違う。二世が災厄の運び手となった時、これを制圧するためだけに誕生した劒冑だ。　祖父の理想を実現する鍵であったあの戒律は、私にとって不要のものだった。
I am not like the first and second generation. I am a tsurugi who was made only to supress the second-generation when she becomes a bringer of calamity. The precept that was the key to realizing grandfather's ideals meant nothing to me.

それでも継いだのは――
And yet, what I inherited was――

善悪相殺の掟は、村正という劒冑の付録ではない。　心鉄に根差すもの、つまり根本理念だ。
The law of counterbalancing good and evil, it is not just an extra to the tsurugi known as Muramasa. It is something rooted within the tsurugi's core, in other words, it is a concept that serves as its foundation.

これを取り除くなら、鍛造行程をすべて見直さなくてはならない。　祖父と母、そして祖母と父。一門の探究の総決算であるそれを、独力で一から立て直さねばならないのだ。
If I want to remove it, I would have to rethink the whole forging process. Grandfather, mother, grandmother, and father. The culmination of my family's research, I would have to completely reformulate it by myself.

できる話ではなかった。
That was something I couldn't do.

仮にできたとしても、そうして造られる劒冑は並の出来で、二世村正の力には抵抗し得ない――〝卵〟に汚染される――であろう。　それでは役目を果たせない。
Even if I were able to do that somehow, the resulting tsurugi would be of mediocre quality, it will not be able to resist the second Muramasa's power―― the "eggs"―― and it will probably be contaminated by it. I wouldn't be able to accomplish my duty if that were the case.

千子村正流の鍛造法で劒冑となり、善悪相殺の戒律を継ぐのは避けられないことだった。　　それは……事実だ、が。
I became a tsurugi using the forging methods of Sengou Muramasa, as such the precept of counterbalancing good and evil could not be avoided. That is a fact... but

しかしそのことを抜きにしても、私の心には、戒律を受け継ぎたい気持ちが確かにあった。　戒律を、一門の理想を継ぎたかった。
even if that wasn't the case, there was something in my heart that wanted to inherit it. The precept, and my family's ideals.

祖父達が悩み苦しみ抜いた末に見つけ出した理想が、無為に散ってゆくのを、許せない思いがあった。〝独善〟の撲滅、争いなき世界への希望を、後の世に伝えても良いだろうと――私はそう思っていたのだ。
I feel like I couldn't just let the ideals that my forefathers found through suffering and hardships dissappear. The eradication of "self-righteousness", the wish for a world free of conflict―― I thought that it might be a good thing to pass it on to the future generations.

……無責任な情念。　……どこまでも自侭な考え。
...An irresponsible desire. ...A selfish thought no matter how you think about it.

どのみち選択の余地がなかった件ではある。　けれどその裏に、そんな甘い願いがあったことを、私は記憶している。
In any case, I had no choice in that matter. But I have always remembered that behind that fact lied a naive wish. 

だから許せない。
That's why I can't forgive myself.

呪いに縛られ、好意や敬意を抱いていた人々に刃で報いてゆく彼の苦悶――その心の断末魔に触れるたび、こうなる可能性からあえて目を背けて安い夢に浸った過去の自分自身が、どうしても許せない。
That anguish, being binded by the curse, people who embraced kindness and honour will be rewarded with the edge of a blade――

「Because of your help, we were able to stop the "eggs" from hatching. It wouldn't have been possible with my strength alone...」

「今更だが……それを認める。　これからも力を貸して欲しい」
「It might be a bit late... but I admit it. I want you to keep lending me your powers.」

《…………》
《…………》

《……》

「善悪相殺。　……成程、人を殺すという事は、善と悪を諸共に断つという事だ。ようやく理解できた……」
「Counterbalancing good and evil... I see, killing a person means cutting off both good and evil. I've finally understood...」

「A musha of justice who fights against evil and defeats it to save the people of the world. And then, after defeating the Silver Star, I may be planning to overthrowing Rokuhara as well. 」

右手の親指に歯を立て、腹を浅く食い破る。　血が溢れ始めたそれを、俺は劒冑へ向けた。
I sank my teeth into the thumb of my right hand and tore a shallow gash in my stomach. The blood began to flow, and I pointed it at the tsurugi.

――この指は、太刀を扱うに欠かせぬ指。
――This finger is indispensable for handling a sword.

《……ぁ……》

おずおずと、劒冑が肢を差し伸ばして応える。　触れる。
Timidly, the tsurugi responded by extending its limb. Touch.

血が甲鉄を染める。
The blood stained the armor.

水晶の鐘を打つような楽が、一度。　俺と村正の間を渡った。
A sound similar to the sounding of a crystal bell rang. It passed between Muramasa and me.

これが――――　　最も簡素で、最も古い、武者正調の帯刀儀礼。
This is―――― the simplest and oldest form of the musha unification ceremony.

ここに縁は結ばれ……　俺と村正は初めて、一騎の武者と成った。
Our destiny has been tied together... For the first time, Muramasa and I have become one musha.

久方ぶりに罷り出た、親王の御前。　俺は何をもさて置いて低頭し、深く謝した。
It's been a while since I've been in the presence of the imperial prince. I put everything aside, bowed, and apologized profusely. 

「舞殿宮殿下。　……先日は多大な迷惑をお掛け致しました。伏してお詫び申し上げます」
「Your highness Maidonomiya... I apologize for the great inconvenience that I have caused the other day. Please accept my sincere apologies.」

「……」
「……」

「ま、ま、景明くん……。　大の男がそんな縮こまったらあかんえ」
「Now, now, Kageaki-kun... An adult man shouldn't shrink back like that.」

御簾の奥で発せられる声に叱責の調子はまるでなく、むしろ宥める風であったが。　己の所業を思えば、なら良かったと安堵もできない。俺は容易に頭を上げられなかった。
The voice from behind the bamboo curtains did not sound reprimanding at all, but rather soothing. But considering what I had done, I couldn't feel relieved. I couldn't raise my head that easily.

「日頃世話になってるのはこっちなんやから。　たまには迷惑のひとつも掛けてくれた方が安心できるくらいやわ」

「……」
「……」

あくまで気楽な様子の親王に、言葉も返せない。
I couldn't say a word in reply to the prince, who seemed to be only taking it easy.

「それが劒冑のためやったっちゅうんやから、見上げたもんやねぇ。　武者の鑑やないか……」

Imperial prince Hachiman said so while clapping his hands. The chief and I unexpectedly looked at each other at the same time.

「It might be better for you to say your greetings to the prison guard. Thanks to him not making a fuss unnecessarily, this incident was able to be taken care off before it got too big.」

それは確かに、礼をせねばならなかった。　まったく俺という男は、多くの人間の手を煩わせながら生きている。
I certainly need to thank him for that. I am truly a man who can't live his life without troubling many people.

今更の自覚というものだろうが……。
It took me a while to realize that...

あれが八幡宮来襲を予告した事は、既に伝えている。　適当な口実を設けて親王には――当然署長にも――遷居して頂くべきだと進言もしておいたが。
I've already told them about the announcement of the attack in Hachiman Shrine. I've also suggested that this announcement would be a good reason for the imperial prince to be moved to another location―― Of course, the chief as well. 

その話か。
So it's about that.

「Are you listening, Kageaki-kun? What I'm about to say must not be said anywhere else...」

ほほほと笑う親王。　だが、その笑いの中にも緊張の成分がある。
The imperial prince let out a hearty laugh. However, within that laugh, there was also a hint of tension. 

余程の話のようだ。　……政治向き、であろうか。やはり。
It seems to be a very important matter. ...As I thought. It must be something political.

しかし、そんな話をわざわざ俺にするとは……？
But then, why would he go out of his way to talk about that with someone like me...?

「近々、八幡宮で奉刀参拝の儀式が行われるのは知っているな」

「……その祭礼の場で――」
「...At that festival――」

牧村さんに挨拶して、署長宅の門をくぐる。　常の事ながら、玄関は勤勉かつ優秀なる家宰の手で万全に清められていた。
After greeting Makimura-san, I passed through the gates of the chief's house. As usual, the entrance had been thoroughly cleansed by the diligent and talented family leader.

自分用にあてがわれている一室へ入り、腰を下ろすや、俺はすぐ八幡宮から持参した紙を広げた。　そうして、黙考を開始する。
I walked into the room that was reserved for me, sat down, and immediately unfolded the paper that I had brought from Hachiman Shrine.　As soon as I sat down, I unfolded the paper that Hachimangu had brought with him and began to ponder in silence. 

「………………」
「………………」

《またしばらくはこっちの家なのね》
《So we're staying in this house again for a while.》

《宮様に、何か仕事でも頼まれた？》

《Don't bother.》

「武家の棟梁にとって鶴岡八幡宮は鬼門の地、そう語られるようにしろと。　……二度となれば、声価も不朽だろうな」
「To a samurai lord, the Hachiman shrine is a place that is akin to Achilles' heel. ...If it is attacked once more, the effects would be everlasting.」 
(TL/n: In the siege of Kamakura, Hachiman shrine was a weak spot.)

源氏長者が八幡宮に詣でて武運隆盛を祈る年例行事、奉刀参拝。　これを、襲い、
The Minamoto clan's chief paid a visit to Hachiman Shrine to pray for their fortune and to perform a ceremony.　They were attacked,  

正三位六衛大将領、元帥竜軍大将、大和の覇者、足利護氏を―――　討つ。
and Ashikaga Moriuji, the third ranked general of the Sixth order, general of the Imperial Army, and Champion of Yamato, was defeated. 
(recheck this later)

「……そして」

「大きく動揺するであろう幕府を朝廷権威で補強してやり――反面、朝廷の発言力を増す。　この公武合体による新体制で官民の対立を緩和、治政に安定をもたらし」
「The shogunate would be greatly shaken, and the authority of the imperial court would reinforce the shogunate―― while at the same time increasing the influence of the imperial court's voice. This cooperation would give birth to a new system that will alleviate antagonism between the government and the people, stabilizing the government's rule.」

「ＧＨＱの介入する隙を無くしてゆく……」
「Thus the opportunity for GHQ to intervene would be eliminated...」

「まとめると、そういうことやねぇ」
「That's the gist of it.」
