「……」

雄略と呼ぶべきだろう。　徒手空拳に等しい身で強大な軍事政権に挑み、その体質を改めさせようというのであるから。
It could be called heroic.　It is an eloquent strategy to challenge a powerful military regime and force it to change its ways.

成就する見込みの程は知れない。　が、何もせず情況を見守れば、進駐軍は時節が到来次第六波羅の排除に乗り出し――これを遂げて大和を完全な占領下に置くか。
There's no telling how likely it is to be accomplished. However, if they only watched and did not act, the Allied Forces will set out to eliminate Rokhala when the time is right―― Let them succeed and have Japan completely under their control...

それとも六波羅が勝利を得て大和唯一の支配権者となりおおせるか。　この国はどちらかの結末を迎えるだろう。……苛烈な交戦の後に。
or have Rokhala emerge victorious as the sole ruler of Yamato. After such a fierce war... which ending will this country greet in the end? 

いや、可能性はもう一つある。　両者の相克に決着がつかず、延々と戦争が続く――という最悪の展開も起こり得る。
No, there is one more possibility. Both sides could not settle their rivalry, and the war will continue to go on forever―― Such a horrible conclusion could also happen. 

喜ばしからざる運命を拒否し、比較的にでも良好な未来を手に入れたいと望むなら、やはり行動は必要だ。　親王と署長、この二人の構想は、暴挙といえば暴挙であったが至当といえば至当に違いなかった。
If they wanted to reject their unpleasant fate and have a relatively better future, they would have to act. The plan of these two men, the prince and the chief, you could say that it was reckless, and yet it was also within reason. 

「どやろ」
「It seems that」

暗殺を実行できる者は、俺しかいない。　足利護氏は戦歴余る武者。銃一丁で倒せるような男ではない。同じ武者だけがその首級を狙える。
I'm the only one who could carry out the assassination. Ashikaga Moriuji is a musha with a long history. He is not the kind of man who can be defeated with a gun. Only another musha can take his head. 

春煕親王は大仰に頭を下げたりしなかった。　大和のため国民のためと、くどく言い重ねることも。
Imperial prince (name later) did not bow down in a grandiose fashion. He also did not try to persuade everyone that he was doing it for the sake of Japan and its people. 

説明は全てした。　後は自分自身の判断で決めろ――そういうことか。
I've explained everything. The rest is up to you to decide for yourself―― That's how it is, huh.

「…………」
「…………」

親王の企図こそ大和を救う。　そう信じるのに、苦労は要らなかった。
The imperial prince plan is to save Yamato. It didn't take much effort to believe that. 

容易な計画ではなかろう。齟齬もあろうし見落としもあろう。きっと困難は多い――が、この人ならばと思わせるものが、親王には確かにあった。　署長という補佐役もいるのだ。
It will not be an easy plan. There may be some failures, and some things may be overlooked. There will definitely be many difficulties―― but there was something about the Prince that made me think that he would be able to do it. He also has the chief as an assistant.  

何より俺の頭では親王のそれに優る計画を思いつかないのだから、価値を否定できる筋合いではなかった。　　親王が間違っているとは、どの角度からも言えない。
Above all, I coulnd't come up with a better plan myself, so I had no reason to deny it. There is no angle in which I could say that the prince was wrong. 

……ならばできるか。　足利護氏を襲い、命を奪えるか。
...Then can I do it? Can I attack Ashikaga Moriuji and take his life? 

（大和のために）
（This is for Yamato.）

多くの善き人々を救うために、　一人の悪しき者を殺す。
Take the life of one evil person in order to save many good people.

…………それは、　　　俺が既に幾度も、幾度も、繰り返してきた所業だ。
...That's something I've done over and over again.

銀星号の拡大を阻止すべく、〝卵〟に寄生された武者を幾人となく斬り殺した。
In order to stop the Silver Star's influence from spreading further, he killed many mushas who were infected by the "Egg". 

一悪を断ち多善を残す。
Cut off one evil and leave many good.

まるで同じだ。　何処にも違いなど無い。
It's the same. There's no difference. 

どちらも、
Both of them

国のため。人のため……　そんな聞こえの良い外面を一枚剥けば、そこに真実の姿が覗く。
are for the good of the country. The good of the people... If you peel back the facade sounds so good, the truth can be seen.

親王の動機が実は私利私欲だとか、間の抜けた事を言うつもりはない。　しかし、対立者を暴力で挫くという道を選ぶのなら、動機がどうあれそれはやはり独善の行いなのだ。
I have no intention on saying that the prince is acting out of his own selfish desires. However, if he is going to choose the path of crushing his opposition with violence, no matter the motive, that is an act of self-righteousness.

我の善のため、　彼の善を悪と称して葬る。　　一剣一殺是善悪相殺。
For my good, I will consider his good as evil. One sword, one kill, that is counterbalancing good and evil.

俺の返答は定まった。
My answer was set in stone.

「行きましょう。　奉刀参拝の日、足利護氏の前へ」
「Let's go. On the day of the ceremony, let us go before Ashikaga Moriuji.」

「……やってくれるんか？」
「...Are you going to do it?」

むしろ意外そうな、親王の声だった。　顔色こそ変えていないが、脇の署長も内心は同じと見える。
The sound of the prince's voice was surprising. Although his expression didn't change, but the chief on the other side of the room seemed to be feeling the same way inside.

俺はかぶりを振った。
I shook my head.

「今はお約束致しかねます」
「I can't promise anything right now.」

「……何？」
「...What?」

「本人と見えてから決します。　斬るか、斬らぬか」
「I will decide once I meet the person himself. 

「足利護氏は殺さねばならない男なのか。　この目で、見て……決めたく思います」
「Whether or not Ashikaga Moriuji is someone that must be killed. I will see with my own eyes... and then decide.」

「…………」
「…………」

「…………」
「…………」

「却って御迷惑とあれば無論、強いて望みは致しません。　ここで聞いた事はすべて忘れ、直ちに立ち去りましょう」
「If this is too much trouble for you, of course I will not force you to do it.　Forget everything you've heard here and leave immediately.」

「如何か――」
「As for――」

「ええよ」
「It's fine.」

「宮殿下……」
「Your highness...」

「計画を打ち明ける段階で、景明くんを信頼するちゅうことは決めてたんや。　ならとことん信じ切ろうやないか」
「I had already decided to trust you when I told you about my plan. So I will trust you all the way.」

「景明くんの判断を信じて、任せるわ」
「I'll trust your judgment, Kageaki-kun. I'll leave it to you.」

「……御高配痛み入ります」
「...Thank you for your generosity.」

「斬ったらあかん、思うたらそれでええ。　その時は、後で景明くんの考えをわしらに聞かせてくれな」
「If you think that he shouldn't be killed, then that's fine. In that case, tell us your thought afterwards, Kageki-kun.」

「はっ」
「Understood]

……過分なまでの信頼を抱かれている。　有難くも、両肩に重かった。
...He has an undue amount of trust in me.　TAlthough I'm thankful for that, it was a heavy weight on my shoulders.

しかも俺は、この信頼に刃で応えなくてはならない。
Moreover, I have to repay this trust with my blade.

「もう一つ、お断りしておかねばならぬ事があります」
「There is one more thing that I have to refuse.」

「うん？」
「Hm?」

「我が劒冑……　村正の掟はご存知であられる筈」
「My tsurugi... Your highness should be aware of Muramasa's law.」

敵を斬らば友も斬らん。
If you kill your enemy, you will also kill your ally.

「…………」
「…………」

「舞殿宮殿下。　もしも自分が、足利護氏を斬った暁には」
「Your highness Maidonomiya. If I were to slay Ashikaga Moriuji,」

「貴方の御命をも頂かねばなりません」
「I would also have to take your life as well.」

それが村正の掟。　善悪相殺の律法。
That is the law of Muramasa. The precept of counterbalancing good and evil.

「宜しいか」
「Is that all right?」

「承知したえ」
「Acknowledged.」

「……」
「……」

「このアホが大将領と差し違えるわけやな。　……大儲けやないか」
「It seems that fool has been mistaken as a great general. ...How unfortunate.」

「わしの代わりなら、何処にでもおるわ」
「You can find a replacement for me anywhere.」

「宮殿下……」
「Your highness...」

嘘の響きは聞き取れなかった。　……それはもしかすると、俺の耳が騙されただけで、親王はいま内心で用が済んだら俺を始末しようと決意しているのかもしれない。
It didn't sound like a lie. ...It could be that my ears are just deceiving me, and that the prince is secretly thinking of getting rid of me when it's all done.

どちらが真実か。　　どちらであっても、舞殿宮春煕親王という人物は、心底からの敬意を払うに値する。
Which is true? Whichever it is, prince Haruki of Maidonomiya is someone who deserves my deepest respect. 

「景明」
「Kageaki」

「はい」
「Yes」

厳しい声に視線を動かす。
I shifted my gaze towards the stern voice.

この人が口を開くことは予測していた。　何を言うのかも。
I had predicted that this person would open his mouth. Perhaps even what he would say.

「その時は私を斬れ」
「Should that time come, slay me.」

「菊池」
「Kikuchi」

「いいな」
「Do you understand? 」

御簾の方を振り返らず、俺だけを見据えて、署長は重石のような声で告げた。　不動の意思がそこにあった。
Without looking back towards the bamboo curtains, the chief said his eyes on me and said so in a gravely voice. His will was unshakable.

――善悪相殺。
――Counterbalancing good and evil.

足利護氏を斬るなら、この人も斬らねばならない。
If I were to kill Ashikaga Moriuji, I would have to kill this person as well.

「署長……」
「Chief...」

「明堯様」
「Akitaka-sama」

何年ぶりにか、養父の名を呼ぶ。　応えはなかった。
For the first time in many years, I called out my adoptive father's name.　There was no response.

……殺せない。　殺せるわけがない。
...I can't kill him. There's no way I could.

大恩あるこの人を、どうして我が手で斬れよう。
How can I cut down this person to whom I owe so much with my own hands?

（だが）
（However)

そう思う一方、足利護氏は構わず斬れるのか。
But at the same time, could I really kill Ashikaga Moriuji without any care?

同じ人間である。　善あり悪あり功あり罪ある、同じ只人である。
He is also human. He is also an ordinary person who has his goods and bads.

単に俺の立つ位置からは署長の善ばかりが、護氏の悪ばかりが目立つというだけに過ぎない。　異なる位置に立つ者には、異なる見方があるだろう。
It's just that from where I stand, I can only see the chief's good sides while Gouji's bad sides stand out. 

なのに一方のみ悪として斬り、もう一方を善として生かすのは、　　――独善である。
But then if I onesidely kill someone because I deemed them to be evil, and let the other live because I deemed them to be good―― that would be an act of self-righteousness.

村正は言った。　独善こそ争いの根源。殺し合いを正当化し、際限もなく続けさせる元凶――と。
Muramasa said so. Self-righteousness is the source of conflict. It justifies killing each other, and it is the main cause as to why it continues endlessly.

そう。　それは、その通りなのだ。
Yes. That's how it is.

「景明」
「Kageaki」

「諒解しました」
「I understand.」

「……」
「……」

「大将領を斬った、その時は……　貴方を」
「Once I kill the general, I will... you」

斬る。
I will kill him.

この養父を斬る。
I will kill my foster father.

斬らねばならぬ。
I have to kill him.

……斬れぬのなら、　足利護氏もまた、斬ってはならないのだ。
...If I can't, I won't be able to kill Ashikaga Moriuji either.

「という次第だ」
「That's how it is.」

《……本当に斬るかどうかはともかく。　その用意はする、っていうこと？》
《...Are you saying that whether or not you're really going to kill him, you're going to prepare for it?》

「そうなる」
「That's the case.」

我が決定ながら、はっきりせぬ話だ。　きっぱり断った方が良かったのかもしれない。
Despite it being my decision, I couldn't be clear about it. Maybe it would have been better if I had refused it outright.

が――
However――

《…………》
《…………》

「どうかしたか」
「Is something wrong?」

蜘蛛の沈黙は、物問いたげだった。　水を向けてみる。
The spider's silence seemed to be interrogative in nature. I turned towards the water.

躊躇うような間を数秒はさんで、金打声が伝わってきた。
After a hesitant pause of a few seconds, a golden voice came through.

《……ね、御堂。　そんな話を断れなかったのは》
《...Hey, Midou. The reason you didn't turn it down》

《この間の……　私の》
《is it because of the other day I...》

「いや」
「No.」

《……》
《……》

「脱獄の件は無関係だ。　それよりも……銀星号の予告が」
「The prison break has nothing to do with it. It's more about... the Silver Star's announcement.」

――――おれは八幡宮へゆく。
――――I will go to Hachiman Shrine.

「お前も聞いていただろう」
「You heard it too right?」

《ええ……》
《Yes...》

「まさか周囲が幕兵で固められる奉刀参拝を狙って現れるとは思えないが……　念のためだ」
「I don't think they're aiming on showing up at the shrine during a ceremony surrounded by soldiers... but just in case.」

「八幡宮に詰めていれば、万一の時に素早く対応できる。　宮殿下の依頼を半端に受けたのは、言ってしまえばそのついでだ」
「If I stay at the Hachiman shrine, I can respond quickly in case of an  emergency. That's the reason why I half-heartedly accepted his highness Maidonomiya's request.」

厳戒警備の中へ潜り込む時点で危険は極まっている。　そのうえ暗殺の狙いが加わっても、これ以上危うくはなりようがない。
It's extremely dangerous trying to sneak into the middle of a highly guarded area. On top of that, there is also the assasination, there's nothing more dangerous than that.

……計算と呼ぶには乱暴な、丼勘定だが。
...It's too rough and sloppy to call it a calculation though.

《…………》
《…………》

「ともかく。　やるやらぬは置いて、策は立てておく必要がある」
「Anyways. Whether we do it or not, we need to have a plan.」

「当日、八幡宮にどう潜り込み、元帥にどう近付くか……。　知恵を貸せ。俺の思案には余る部分もある」
「On that day, how can we sneak into Hachiman shrine, and how do we approach the general... Lend me your wisdom. There's more than I can think of.」

《……う、うん》
《...Y-Yeah》

広げていた紙を、村正の方へ向ける。　そうしなくては見えないということもあるまいが、鉄の蜘蛛は天井から降りて近寄ってきた。
I turned the paper I had spread out towards Muramasa. The iron spider descended from the ceiling and approached it, since it would not be able to see it otherwise.

その紙に、親切な表題などはない。　しかし、それが何であるかは一目で知れた筈だ。
That paper did not have any title. But you could tell what it was with just a glance.

《八幡宮の地図？》
《Is this the map of Hachiman shrine?》

「ああ。　宮殿下の直筆だ」
「Yeah. His highness drew it himself.」

《……なんか、おかしくない？》
《...Isn't it a little weird?》

そう言うのは、舞殿宮の作画能力に対する疑問ではないだろう。　地図は素人図面には違いないが、そこそこの正確さで描かれている。
Saying that did not mean she was questioning Maidonomiya's abilitiy to draw. The map is no doubt drawn by an amateur, but it was drawn with a fair degree of accuracy.

その地図と一般に公開されている境内図とでは幾つか大きく異なる部分があり、村正が指摘しているのはそちらだった。
There were some major differences between that map and the publicly available map of the temple grounds, and that was what Muramasa was pointing out.

《これは本殿よね？》
《This is the main shrine, right?》

「そうだ」
「That's right.」

大階段を登った上にある社。　上宮と呼ばれる。
The shrine is located at the top of a large staircase.　It is called the Jouguu (Upper Palace).

《その奥にある……これは何？》
《There's something at the back... What's this?》

「隠された裏参道だそうだ。　ぐるりと回って、地下へ向かう」
「They said it's a hidden path. If you go around, you can head for the basement.」

《……その先の広間は？》
《...And the spacious room beyond that?》

「下宮だ」
「It's the Geguu (Lower Palace). 」

《下宮はこっちでしょう？》
《Isn't the Geguu supposed to be over here?》

「それは若宮。　若宮も下宮と呼ばれるが、本当はこちらを指すらしい」
「That's the Wakamiya. The Wakamiya is also called Geguu, but it seems the real one is this one.」

上宮の真下の、地下空間を指差して言う。　そんなものが存在するなどと、俺もつい先刻聞いて知ったばかりだ。
I said as I pointed at the underground space underneath the upper palace. I've only just now learned of the existence of such a thing.

限られた祭事の折にしか開かれない施設で、公には秘されている、との話であった。
I was told that it was a facility that was only open on limited occasions, and that it was kept secret from the public.

「奉刀参拝の手順だが……　参拝そのものは、大将領と十人余りの側近だけで行われる」
「About the sword offering ceremonial procedures... The ceremony itself will only be performed by the general and his entourage of 10 people.」

「普陀楽から八幡宮までは相当数の兵を引き連れて来るが、彼らは祭祀に関与しない。　徒士衆は敷地の外、武者衆は境内や上空で警備につく」
「They will bring a considerable number of soldiers with them from Fudaraku to Hachiman Shrine, but they will not be involved in the rituals.　The toushis will be outside the grounds, and the mushas will be on guard inside the grounds.」

《……》
《……》

「大将領と側近は上宮へ向かう。　そこで太刀を奉納、祭儀を執り行う」
「The general and his entourage will head towards the upper palace. There, the will offer up the sword and perform the ritual.」

「ここまで襲撃の隙はない」
「There are no openings to make an attack so far.」

《大銀杏の陰に隠れてってわけにはいかないのね》
《There's also no way you can hide behind the large ginkgo tree, is there》

「実朝公の時は本人も随員も非武装であったから、公暁はそれで成功したがな。　護氏が連れる側近のうち少なくとも半数は武者だと云う」
「In the case of Lord Sanetomo, both he and his entourage were unarmed, so Kugyō (Minamoto no Yoshinari) was successful because of that. But among all the aides that accompanied Moriuji, at least half of them are mushas.」


不意を襲っても彼らに防がれるだろう。　そうこうする間に周辺から警備の者が集まってきて、取り囲まれ、終わりだ。
Even if we ambush them they would probably block it. Then when we are making our escape, guards from the surrounding area will surround us, and it would be over.

「しかし、この後。　護氏は供奉の者と別れ、地下へ向かう」
「But after this, Moriuji will part ways with his attendants and head to the basement.」

《……》
《……》

「秘密の下宮にも太刀を奉納するためだ。　同行を許されるのは、祭祀を行う神官数名だけ」
「It's to offer up the sword in the secret Lower Palace as well. The only one who is allowed to accompany him would be a few priests who will perform the ritual.」

《護衛はなし？　……また随分と、おあつらえ向きね》
《No escorts? ...That's surprisingly ideal.》

「これが古くからの慣例で、変更はできないらしい」
「It's apparently an old custom that can't be changed.」

達て望めば変えられなくもないのだろうが、それでは臆病者の謗りを受ける。　身内の信望を失い、四公方の誰かに地位を奪われるような事態になりかねない。
It could be changed if he strongly requested so, but then he will receive critism for being a coward. He will lose the confindence of his people and his position as one of the four lords might be stolen by someone else.

六波羅元帥がそんな運命を良しとするとは考えられなかった。
There was no way that general Rokhara would approve of such a fate.

「暗殺の機会があるとすれば、この下宮参拝の時だけだ」
「The only chance for an assassination would be during the ceremony on the Lower Palace.」

《でしょうね……》
《It seems so...》

「問題は」
「The problem is」

ここから先の具体案。
The planning from here on out.

事前に下宮へ潜んで待つのは難しい。　参拝儀式に先立って境内全域の検査が行われ、危険要素はこの段階で徹底的に洗い出される。それが完了すれば警備網が敷かれ、以後の潜入は不可能となる。
It is difficult to hide and wait in the lower shrine beforehand. The entire premise will go through an inspection before the ceremony starts, and any dangerous elements would thoroughly identified at this stage. A security network will be set up once the inspections are done, attemps of inflitration will be impossible hereafter.

儀式中の強行突入などは論外だ。
Forcible entry during the ceremony is out of the question.

「……やはり手は一つか」
「...I guess there's only one way.」

《神官になりすまして、大将領と一緒に下宮へ降りる？》
《Disguise yourself as a priest and go down to the lower palace together with the general?》

「ああ」
「Yeah.」

そして暗殺を遂げた場合には、すぐさま八幡宮から脱出。これに手管は要らず、騎航での強行突破で良い。　外からの敵襲に備えた警備網は内からの奇襲に即応しかねるだろう。捕まる危険はごく低い筈だった。
Should the assassination proved to be successful, immediately make an escape from Hachiman shrine. No tricks are needed for this, we can just force our way through. The security network that had been prepared for an enemy attack from the outside would not be able to respond immediately to a surprise attack from the inside. The risk of being caught should be very low.

《そうね。　……問題はなさそうだけど》
《Yeah. ...There doesn't seem to be any problems, but》

《何を悩んでるの？》
《What are you worried about?》

「お前をどうするかだ」
「What I'm going to do with you.」

護氏は武者。　もしも挑むことになるなら、劒冑がなくては勝負にならない。
Moriuji is a musha. If you were to challenge him, you would need a tsurugi or else it can't even be called a fight.

のだが……
But...

「持ち込む方法が思いつかん」
「I can't think of a way to bring you in.」

《……私だけ、あらかじめ潜伏しておくってのは駄目なの？》
《...Is it not possible for me to hide in advance?》

「事前検査には武者も加わるそうだ。　如何にお前が隠形に優れていても、武者の信号探査や熱源探査まで騙すのは無理だろう」
「It seems mushas will also participate for the inspection. No matter how good you are at concealment, you won't be able to fool a musha's signal detection and heat source detection.」

《…………。　検査が済んだ後で潜り込もうとしても……同じことよね？》
《...Trying to sneak in once the inspections are done would... lead to the same thing, huh?》

「警備隊に武者がいない筈はないからな……」
「Yeah, since there's no way the guards won't have a musha in their ranks...」

《祭具の中に紛れ込むとか》
《How about blending in with the ritual equipments?》

「無理だろう。　鏡や玉と一緒に蜘蛛の彫像があったら普通気付く。奇天烈過ぎる。文化的に有り得ん」
「That won't be possible. People would usually realize it if a statue of a spider were mixed in with a mirror or a jade. It's too odd. It's culturally impossible.」

《……私、貴方の家で五百年ばかり、鏡や玉と一緒に御神体やってたんですけど》
《...I've been a deity in your house for 500 years along with mirrors and jades though.》

「…………そうだったな」
「...You did.」

振り返れば、奇天烈に過ぎる祭祀であった。
In retrospect, the ritual was too bizarre to be true.

つまるところ、考えはここで渦を巻く。　俺一人の潜入なら神官を装えば済む話だが、村正を連れてとなるともう一工夫が要る――しかし良い案が浮かばない。

The path was not very wide, it was the same for the height. The general and his horse, Muramasa and I who were posing as priests, we were the only ones moving, but the reason why we were so excessively loud was because our footsteps reverberated in this narrow space.

もしもこの中で数十人からの人間が一斉に駆け回りでもしたなら、相当耳に悪いことになりそうだ。

Waiting for my decision.

This man is strong. Physically. Mentally. In every sense of the word.

That strength comes from arrogance. It is most likely supported by a simple desire.

支配欲の権化か。
A lust for control.

しかし、それをもって彼に大和の統治者たるの資格無しとは言えない。　清く正しく道義に生きる者が上に立てば国は治まる――と信じ込むほど俺も夢見がちではなかった。
However, this does not mean that he is not qualified to rule Yamato. I am not so dreamy to believe that the country will definitely be at peace if it was ruled by a pure and righteous man.

理想のみあって力足らぬ王は、むしろ国を乱す。　東西の歴史を紐解けば、その種の前例は枚挙に暇がない。
A king who only has ideals but not enough power will rather throw the country into disorder. The history from both east and west are replete with precedents of this kind.

足利護氏は力に満ち溢れている。　この背は大和全土全国民の命運も、重しとはしないだろう。
Ashikaga Moriuji is full of power. His back will not be weighed down even by the fate of all the people of Yamato.

如何に彼が強欲極まる暴君であろうと――　その両腕の抱え込む大和が、結果的に守られるのであれば。
It doesn't matter how greedy and tyrannical he may be - as long as the Yamato he holds in his arms is protected in the end.

In the end, is he right or wrong as a ruler?

It is a certain fact that the burden on the people has increased greatly under the Rokhara regime. The repression against dissidents is also much more blatant and severe than before.

が。　よって六波羅の統治は悪政だ――と決め付けるのは一概視が過ぎよう。
However, assuming that the reign of Rokhara was bad from that alone may mean that one is only looking at the surface.

情勢というものも併せて評価せねばならない。
The evaluation must be done with the current circumstances considered.

六年前、六波羅は途方もない裏切りを行い、国家を売り、大戦に幕を引いた。そして大和の政権を得た。　だがもし、六波羅が裏切らず、連盟軍と本土決戦を繰り広げていたら？　国土は焦土と化さなかったか？
Six years ago, Rokhara committed a outrageous betrayal. He sold his country and drew the curtains to the great war, thus gaining political authority of Yamato. However, what if Rokhara did not commit that betrayal and had fought in the mainland decisive battle against the Allied Forces? Would the land not have been turned into scorched earth?

六波羅幕府は手本のような軍国主義を敷いており、国民一人一人の権利は全く軽視されている。　だがこの軍国主義体制がなかったら？　大陸情勢の混迷が大和にも波及する可能性はなかったろうか？
The Rokhara shogunate has set an exemplary militaristic system where the rights of individual citizens are totally disregarded. But what if this militaristic system did not exist? Would there not have been a possibility that the chaos currently happening throughout the continent could spread to Yamato as well?

世界的に見て調和の時代とは言い難いこの六年間を、六波羅は曲がりなりにも平穏に――少なくとも他国と交戦することだけはなく――乗り切っているのだ。　過去の体制で同じことができたかはわからない。
Looking at it from a global perspective, in the six years that could hardly be said as an age of harmony―― although imperfect―― at the very least Rokhara did not engage in warfare with other countries, but only sought to weather through it peacefully. That might not have been possible under the past regime. 

百年後の歴史家は、六波羅の統治を「最善の手法」として評価するのかもしれなかった。
A hundred years from now, historians might praise Rokhara's rule as the "best method".

（……そんな教科書を読みたくはないが……）

六波羅幕府の暴虐を目の当たりしている現代大和人の多くは、俺と感想を同じくするだろう。　しかし後世の視点に立てば、つまり客観視に徹すれば、そのような評価もきっと下せるのだ。
If the people of modern Yamato were to witness the tyranny of the Rokhara shogunate before their eyes, many of them will probably share my opinion. However, if we look at it from the perspective of future generations, which means looking at is with a thoroughly objective point of view, such an evaluation can be made.

今、足利護氏を抹殺し。　六波羅体制に終止符を打つ――

「It pains me to stain the treasures of the Minamoto clan with the blood of common soldiers.　Out of respect for your courage to aim for my neck, I shall give you a taste of a blade so sharp it cuts through water.」

「帰命頂礼八幡大菩薩！　我、御器と罷り成る!」
「Return to life, Great Bodhisattva Hachiman! I shall serve as your humble servant!」

「御堂！」
「Midou!」

……逃げ道はない。　俺個人にはともかく、舞殿宮には。
...There is no escape path. Not for me personally, but for Maidonomiya.

既にこちらの正体は割れているのだ。　大将領を生かして帰せば、親王は罪を問われ、無為の死を遂げるだろう。
Our identities have been found out. If we let the general return alive, the prince will accused of a crime and will die a fruitless death.

最早これまで。　覚悟を決めるしかない！
This is it. We have to prepare ourselves!

足利護氏を……斬る!　　そして――――
I will slay Ashikaga Moriuji! And then――――

「その時は私を斬れ」
「Should that time come, slay me.」

「いいな」
「Got it?」

「――――村正ァッ!」
「――――Muramasa!」

「そちらは蝦夷の女であったか……。　うまく装束で隠していたな」
「So that one was an Emishi woman... You hid it well with your disguise.」

「But even if you show yourselves, what can you do?」

「決まってるでしょ」
「Isn't that obvious?」

「We're going to have a sword fight with the bearded swordsman's armor.」

「……」

「……」

「...Hey, Midou. Leaving him aside, why are you also looking at me with a "what is this woman talking about" face?!」

「す、済まん。　お前のその格好を見ていると、未だにピンと来ないものが――」
「S-sorry. Looking at this form of yours, there's something I still can't quite put my finger on.」

「The truth of the Tsurugi is here!」

「………………」
「………………」

《なに？》
《What?》

「いや……」
「It's nothing...」

奇妙な安堵を得て、苦笑する。
I chuckle with a strange sense of relief. 

装甲してみてわかった。　　……村正は別に何も変わっていない。
I understood when I armored up. ...There's nothing different about Muramasa.

俺の劒冑だ。
It's my tsurugi.

見てくれに惑わされて悩む必要などなかったのだ。
There's no need for me to be bothered by appearances.

「――Let's go!」

《諒解！》
《Understood!》

「むっ――」
「Mmph――」

噛み合った初太刀と初太刀。　それは宙空に火花を散らし、互いの腕に撃衝を走らせた。
The swords clashed. It created a spark in the air and sent shockwaves through both our arms.

重い。　……だが、ほぼ互角か。
Heavy. ...But I guess we're about even. 

こちらが喉奥で唸るのと同時、大将領も忌々しげな鼻息を洩らしていた。
As I let out a groan from the back of my throat, the general also let out an abhorrent grunt.

「見掛け倒しではないようだな……」
「Looks like you're not just for show...」

「殿下にお褒め頂けるとは光栄の極み」
「Being praised by his highness has always been my greatest honor.」

「若造が。　何処の産か知らんが、腕相応に眼も養っておけというのだ」
「You greenhorn. I don't know where you're from, but you need to develop your eyes as well as your arms.」

「さすれば舞殿宮如きの飼い犬で一生を棒に振ることもなかったろうよ」
「If you had, you wouldn't have spent your whole life in the clutches of a dog like Maidonomiya.」

「生憎、眼力を養っていれば尚のこと、貴方のもとで禄を食む道は選べなかったであろうと存ずる」
「Unfortunately, if I had developed my eyesight, that is all the more reason I wouldn't choose the path of earning a stipend under you.」

「抜かすわ！」
「You sure can talk!」

怒声を発し、踏み込んでくる敵騎。　その挙措、太刀取りは六波羅新陰流のそれ――但し自己流の崩れが随所に見られる。
The enemy approaches while shouting angrily. His behavior and stance are that of the Rokuhara Shinkage-ryu (Japanese fencing), but it can be seen that he completely changed it into his own style.

この将帥が戦に古りている証であろう。　齢六十に迫る筈だが、鈍さはまるで窺えない。
It is a sign that the general aged in the battlefield. He must be close to sixty years old, but there  no sign of dullness.

敵騎の鋭鋒を迎えるに、頼れるのは刀法のみだった。　半球に近い形状の地下空間は、学校がひとつ収まるほどの広さと高さを備えるが、それでも武者が騎航術の粋を競う場としては全く足りない。
The only thing that could be relied upon to face the sharp edge of the enemy was the sword method.　The semi-spherical underground space was about as large and tall as a school, but it was still not enough for mushas to compete to the utmost of their abilities.

壁面に激突する醜態を望まないなら、地面に足裏をつけて戦う一択である。
If you don't want to end up crashing into a wall, you have to fight with your sole on the ground.

「ふッ……」
「Hmph...」

「!」


「チ――」
「Guh――」

曲技を！　上段から斬り下ろすと見せかけて変化、手元へ引き込んだ太刀を一直線に突き出してきた。
A feign! He made it look like he was going to slash down from the top, but instead he changed and thrust out his sword in a straight line, pulling it into his hand.

俺の反応が後僅かにでも遅れていたら、喉仏を貫かれていただろう。　対手はやはり、相当に場慣れしている。
If I had reacted even a little bit later, my throat would have been pierced. My opponent is definitely quite experienced.

（……しかし）
（...However)

良く体捌きが間に合ったものだと、俺は刹那、他人事のように感心した。　従来の己であれば避けられなかったろうと思う。
I was impressed for a moment, as if it were someone else's problem, that I had been able to dodge that on time.　If I was still the old me, I don't think I would have been able to avoid it.

今日は動きが軽い。
My movement is light today.

甲鉄が肌に合う。　微妙な違和感さえも今はなく、本当に肉体と同一化してしまったように感じている。
The armor fits my body. Even the subtle feeling of discomfort is gone now, and I feel as if we have truly become one.

正当の帯刀を行った成果か。
I guess it's the result of doing a proper tsurugi equipment ceremony.

これが真の意味で武者になるという事か！
So this is what it means to be a true musha!

《想像通り、敵の劒冑は大した物よ。　けれど、想像以上ってことはない》
《As I thought, the enemy's tsurugi is quite impressive. But it's not stronger than what I imagined.》

《村正なら勝てる！》
《If it's us, we can win!》

「肯！」
「Yeah!」

「端武者がッ!」
「You common soldier!」

「推参!」
「Here I go!」

剣の軌道が交差し、刃金と刃金は弾き合う。　　が――これは俺の想定の内！
The swords' trajectories crossed, and the two steels repelled each other. But - this was within my expectations!

「む?」
「Hngh?」

弾かれた太刀をそのまま、頭上でぐるりと取り回し。　……対称の形で再び襲う！
As the sword repelled, I handled it and spinned it above my head. ...I attacked once again with a symmetrical blow!

吉野御流合戦礼法、木霊打ち。
Yoshino imperial battle etiquette, Kodama-uchi. 

「きッ……貴様ァ!」
「Y-You bastard!」

肩口に刀痕を深々と刻まれ、六波羅元帥が短く憤怒を叫ぶ。
With a sword scar etched deep into his shoulder, general Rokhara briefly shouted in anger.

首筋を狙って打ち込んだのだが……　咄嗟に身を捻って最も甲鉄が厚い箇所で受けるとは、流石。
I aimed at his neck and struck... but to think he would quickly turn around to accept the blow where his armor was thickest, as expected of him I guess. 

《でもあの肩、もう一太刀加えれば破れる》
《But with one more strike, that shoulder can be cracked.》

「……させてはくれまいがな」
「...I don't think he'll let us hit it though.」

太刀を取り直して呟く。　自分自身の油断を戒めるためでもあった。
I muttered as I gripped my sword. It was also to warn myself against being careless.

敵騎は怒りに双眸を滾らせながら、しかしやや遠間になった距離を保っている。　戦闘方針を猛進から慎重へと大きく切り替えた様子だ。
The enemy's eyes are bulging with anger, and yet he still maintains a slight distance. It seems their battle plan has changed from rushing ahead to being cautious.

勢い任せの猪突は最早するまい。　こちらも対応して意識を改めておかないと、思わぬ不覚を取る羽目になりそうである。
He will no longer recklessly charge on impulse. We must also change our mindset in response to that, otherwise we might end up making an unforseen mistake.

どう出るか。
How is he going to attack?

見るに、対手は俺の出方を待つ構えだ――が、気質を思えばただ待ち続けということはなかろう。　待つ一方で、攻め手を探っているに違いない。
From how it looks, it seems that he is waiting for me to make a move, but considering his temperament, I don't think he will just keep waiting. While waiting, he must also be looking for a way to attack.

そして俺は俺で、手堅く地道な戦術に徹してばかりはいられない事情があった。　戦闘の長期化は危険なのだ。
As for me, I came to a situation where I can't just keep persisting in using straightforward tactics. Prolonging this battle is dangerous.

いつまでも大将領が戻らなければ、地上で待機する幕府の士卒は異常事態の発生を悟る。　武者を一隊、送り込んでくるだろう。
If the general doesn't return after quite some time, the officers waiting above ground will realize that something is amiss. They will most likely send in a group of mushas.

そうなっては俺の命運も窮まる。
If it comes to that, I'm doomed. 

「……っ」


胸の震えを、呼気にして押し出した。　焦ってはならない……。
I pushed out the trembling in my chest as I exhaled. I musn't panic...

相手は練達の武者だ。　一度の不覚が文字通り命取りになる。
The opponent is a skilled musha. One slip-up will be fatal. 

まずは、誘いの術を掛けてみるか。　それで釣れれば良し、釣れなくとも――
First of all, let's try to lure them in.　If it works, good. If not...

《え?》
《Huh?》

心臓が一回、鼓動を飛ばした。　前触れもなしの轟音。
My heart skipped a beat.　A roar without warning.

合当理だ。　敵騎が――合当理に火を入れている。
It's the Gattari. There's fire coming out of the opponent's Gattari.
(tl/n: Gattari --> banner mounting at the back of samurai armor)

（真逆）
（No way）

……騎航するつもりか?　この限られた空間で！
...Is he trying to take off? In this confined space?!

「思い出してきたわ……」
「I'm starting to remember...」

「……？」
「……？」

「戦場の風。　噎せ返るような屍臭」
「The winds of war. The suffocating smell of corpses.」

「That repulsive smell...」

――――飛び立った、
He took off.

（無茶を）
（He's being reckless)

焦りに負けたのか。　これは、どう計っても自殺行為……
He gave in to impatience. This is suicide no matter how you look at it. 

敵騎の姿が消えるのと、ほとんど同瞬に襲ってきた一刀を危うく打ち返す。　正確に首根を狙っていたその太刀筋に、皮膚が総毛立った。
As the enemy disappeared, I barely returned the strike that came towards me at about the same moment. It was a very precise strike to the base of the neck, and the strike made my skin crawl.

しかし、この先は――　敵騎は壁に突入して、己の墓穴を掘るしかない筈、
But from here on out, the enemy would have no choice but to charge into the wall and dig their own grave... 

「何だとォ?」
「What the-?」

有り得ぬ光景が顕現した。
An unbelievable scene manifested itself.

猛スピードで壁に突き進んだ敵騎が、刹那、騎体を反転させ。　対面効果も利用し、勢力を絶妙に殺す……
The enemy, which has been plunging towards the wall at great speed, changed directions in an instant. By utilizing the fact that we were face-to-face, he perfectly killed off his momentum... *check again

そして両脚で壁を蹴り。　再び、俺目掛けて襲い来る!
Then he kicks the wall with both legs. And again, he set his sights on me and attacked. 

《冗談でしょぉっ?》
《You're kidding, right?》

完全に意表を突かれては、躱しきるのも無理だった。　胸甲に刃先を浴びる。
It was impossible to dodge when you were caught completely off guard. The tip of the blade hit my breastplate.

寸前で上体を反らし、浅傷に留めるのが精々の限度。　反撃などしている暇はなかった。
He was able to turn his body around just in time and only sustain a minor injury.　There was no time for a counterattack.

……夢だと思いたいところだが、夢ではない。　異常も異常、無道法外の騎体運動を、敵は実現している！
...I would like to think that it's just a dream, but it's not. The enemy just did an extraordinary and outrageous move.

「縦回転ができるような騎体かっ?」
「It's capable of doing a Kulbit?」
(tl/n: Kulbit --> an aerial maneuver where an aircraft performs an extremely tight loop, often not much wider than the length of the aircraft itself.)

「貴様が洟を垂らしていた頃の、大陸の戦で……石窟寺院に立て篭もって敵の軍勢を迎え撃ったことがあった」
「While you were snivelling, there was a time when I confined myself in a cave temple to intercept an enemy army.」

「これはその折に編み出した技術よ。　若造がッ、どう背伸びしても届くまい！」
「This is a technique I developed at that time. No matter how much you push yourself, you won't be able reach it lad!」

「あ、あの大将軍……　実は〝赤い悪魔〟戦団の出身ではなかろうな」
「T-That general... he's not actually from from the Freiherr Flying Circus, is he?」

《余裕っぽいこと言ってる場合かな》
《Is it really the time to be saying such carefree things?》

全く違う。
It's completely different.

片や騎航、片や徒行では、速力に差がつき過ぎる。　後者唯一の利点であり、本来ならこの空間において大きく意味をなす筈の小回りは、敵手の常軌を逸した曲芸技でほぼ無効化されてしまった。
There is too much of a gap between his flying speed and ground speed. The latter could be the only advantage I have against him. Originally, the tight turns in this empty space would be of great significance, but even that has been nullified by his unorthodox acrobatics.

このままでは何もできずに斬り刻まれる。
If I don't do anything, I'll be cut to pieces.

これで三度。　……どうにか決定打は避けているが、運にせよ技量にせよいつまでも続くまい。
This is the third time. ...I managed to avoid his decisive blow somehow, but whether that was luck or skill, it wouldn't last forever.

敵騎の運動が速過ぎ、奇想天外過ぎて、対応の手が完全に遅れてしまう。　反撃、迎撃が実行できないのだ。
The enemy's movement is too fast and unreadable, anything I have to equal him will definitely not be fast enough. I can't counterattack nor intercept.

一方的に攻め立てられるばかりでは、つまり敗北が時間の問題である。
If he one-sidedly keeps up his onslaught, our defeat will be a matter of time.

（どう……する？）
（What should... I do?）

無理矢理にでも手を出すか？　しかし、それが致命的な隙を生めばそこまでとなる勝負。
Should I make a move even if I have to force myself? However, if that gives birth to a fatal gap in my defences, that will be the end of the battle. 

ならこちらも騎航して――それこそ最悪の下策だ。　俺にあんな芸当はできない。今日が初騎航の騎士のように蝶々泳ぎをするのが関の山。
Then we'll fly too―― That's the worst possible plan. I can't pull off such a stunt. The most I could do would be to do a butterfly stroke, just like a pilot on his first day of flight. 
(tl/n: butterfly stroke is one of the hardest swimming strokes. he is probably saying that the best he could do is to struggle trying to do what the enemy did.)

宙に浮く分、今より状況が悪化する。　敵騎は墜落を避けるため、攻撃の際は必ず水平騎航で来るが、俺が地面から離れればその制約も必要なくなるからだ。
If I was in the air, the situation would be worse than it is right now. The enemy always comes in horizontally when attacking to avoid crashing, but if I leave the ground, that limitation will be lifted.

どちらの選択も分が悪過ぎる。　だが――しかし……。
Both choices are way too bad. But―― But...

《……御堂！》
《...Midou!》

「村正？」
「Muramasa?」

「往生際の良からぬ奴。　潔く首を差し出せば、綺麗に刎ねてやろうものを！」
「You really don't know when to give up. If you had just quietly offered up your neck, I would have chopped it off cleanly!」

「……」
「……」

「寸刻みの方が好みなら、そうしてくれるわ」
「If you prefer it to be cut off bit by bit, then I shall do that for you.」

「――――」
「――――」

（何？）
（What?）

（生身――　劒冑を捨てた？）
（In the flesh―― He abandoned his tsurugi?）

（馬鹿な。　何を企む）
（This is absurd. What is he up to?

（どうする）
（What should I do?）

（一度騎航を止めるか）
（I should maybe stop flying for a bit.）

（――いや）
（―― No.）

（それが狙いか！）
（So that's what he's aiming for!）

（奇策でこちらを地上に戻し、勝負を仕切り直そうと）
（He's acting strangely to try to lure me back on the ground and start this match all over again.）

（乗るかッ!）
（There's no way I'll go along with that!）

「そんな浅知恵に――」
「To such shallow wisdom――」

「乗ったな。大将領」
「You fell for it, general.」

「?」


「な――――ッ」
「Gah――――」

《蜘蛛の巣へようこそ。　……一瞬の躊躇さえ無ければ、貴方の勝ちだったのにね！》
《Welcome to the spider's web. ... If only you hadn't hesitated for a moment, you would have won!》

村正の糸に、甲鉄を切り裂くまでの強度はない。　しかし絡め取った敵騎の母衣に損傷を与え、地表へ引き摺り落とすには充分であった。
Muramasa's thread was not strong enough to cut through the armor. However, it was enough to damage the enemy's cloak(rocket), thus dragging him down to the ground.

最高速力で疾駆していたわけではない。被害程度も再起不能には遠いだろうが、性能を大きく失った状態にあることは確実。　村正発案の一策は成功した。
It was not running at top speed. The degree of damage would be far from irreversible, but it was certain that it had lost much of its performance.　Muramasa's plan was a success.

この機を捉える。
I must seize this chance.

再び装甲。　驚くべき強靭さで早くも立ち上がろうとしている敵に向かい、跳躍する。
I armoured up again. I leap towards the enemy, who to my surprise, is already tenaciously trying to get up. 

「御免！」
「Sorry!」

「ぬぅ!」
「Ngh!」

手応え――は、土！　地面に身を投げ出して、対手は太刀先を躱していた。
His response was―― the ground! By throwing himself to the ground, he managed to dodge his opponent's sword.

百万軍の大将にあるまじき姿と嗤うより、ただただその執念に戦慄する。　一撃は必殺だった――しかし足利護氏の生存と勝利への渇望が殺意を上回った。そうとしか思われない。
Rather than laughing at the shameful sight from a general of a million troops, I simply shuddered at his persistence. This blow should have brought certain death―― but Ashikaga Moriuji's desire for survival and victory exceeded my intent to kill. That's all I can think of.

何たる男か。
What a guy.

怯えに近いものさえ感じつつ、足は止めない。　転がって逃げる敵騎を追い、その立ち上がる出端に一刀を加える。
Even while feeling something close to fear, his feet did not stop. I chase after the enemy as he scatters about, aiming to deliver a single strike while he is still trying to stand up.

再び、縦―― と見せて横へ薙ぐ。
Again, vertically―― make him think that but actually hit him from the side.

「くッ!」
「Guh!」

胸甲を割り裂く刃先。　細かい金属粒が無数、仄かに煌いて虚空を彩る。
The edge of the blade splits the breastplate. A myriad of fine metal particles glittered faintly, coloring the empty space.

だが……浅い！
But... it's still shallow!

敵騎は咄嗟に飛び下がっていた。　避け切れぬと悟った瞬間、利き足で地面を蹴って。
The enemy jumped back as quickly as possible. The moment he realized that he could not avoid it, he kicked the ground with his dominant foot.

……どこまでも！
...I'll chase you anywhere!

距離が空く。
There was distance between us.

敵騎が太刀を構え直す。
The enemy readied his sword once more.

（取り逃がしたか）
（I missed my chance)

仕留めの機は失われた。　深入りは既に危険――逆撃で報いられる。
I lost my chance to deliver the last blow. Trying to go in at this point is too dangerous―― I will just be greeted with a counterattack.

決着をつけてしまいたかったが、仕方ない。
I wanted to end the battle then, but it can't be helped.

《大丈夫。風向きは変わってる。　こっちの追い風よ》
《It's okay. The winds have changed. It is in our favour.》

「つんのめって転ぶのだけ気をつけておけということだな」
「I guess that means I have to be careful not to fall.」

こちらとて手傷は負っているが、今は敵騎の損害の方が激しい。　油断さえしなければ、力で押し込んでいける。
We are wounded, but the damage to the enemy is more severe now. As long as we're not careless, we can bring them down.

前方、左右に足を進め、打ち込む間合を計る。　しかし敵も然る者、いちいち巧妙に間を外す。
I moved my left leg forward, followed by the right, trying to get into striking distance. But the enemy is formidable, he never lets me close the distance.

戦闘経験では先方に分が有るせいか、埒が明かない。
Perhaps it was because the opponent had the advantage in combat experience, but we couldn't make any progress.

「…………」
「…………」

「…………」
「…………」

ここまで来て、時間切れ――敵側の来援という結末は願い下げだった。　一撃受けるのを覚悟して、一気に攻め出るべきか。数秒、脳裏で考えを弄ぶ。
Having come this far, I didn't want to run out of time and end up having to face the enemy reinforcements as well. Should I just prepare myself to take a blow or should I launch an attack? I played with the idea for a few seconds in my mind.

……計算上、俺にとって悪い勝負とは言えない。　が、
...According to my calculations, it's not really a bad match for me. However,

（村正。　あの劒冑の底をどの程度と見積もる？）
（Muramasa. How strong do you think is that tsurugi's bottom armour?）

《私とほぼ互角の甲鉄。反則物の機動性。　……これでおしまい、って考えるのは虫が良過ぎるんじゃないかしら》
《It's armour quality is about equal to mine. It has an unfair amount of mobility. ...Thinking that this is the end of the list might be asking for too much.》

（まだ、有るか）
（So there's still more, huh.）

《鬚切といえば、神代とまでは言わないにしても上古の作……誰がどんな技術で鍛えたのかも知られていない古代遺産よ。　何が飛び出してくるやら》
《Speaking of Higekiri, although you can't say that it was made during the age of gods, it is still a creation from ancient times... It is an ancient legacy in which who or how it was made is unknown. Of all the things that could pop out.》

《最低限、陰義のことは考えておくべきね。　知りたかったのはそこでしょう？》
《At the very least, you should bear its shinogi in mind. That's what you wanted to know, right?》

（ああ）
（Yeah)

陰義。　武者戦の計算外要素……計算を根底から覆し得る力。
Shinogi. An unaccounted factor within a battle of mushas... A power that can overturn any calculations from its roots.

追い込まれた敵騎が恃むとすれば、まずこれだろう。　おそらく今は、実行の機を窺っているのだ。
This is the first thing that a cornered enemy rider would rely on. Perhaps they are now looking for an opportunity to activate it.

勝負を決めようと踏み込んだ途端、待ち構えていたそれに迎え撃たれる可能性もある。
As soon as you step in to decide the battle, you may be intercepted by it that has been lying in wait.

《いっそこちらから仕掛ける？》
《Should we attack first?》

村正が言うのは、同様の手段で先手を打て、ということだ。　――こちらが先に、陰義で仕掛ける。
Muramasa was saying to take the first move while using a similar ability. ――We will attack first with our shinogi.

しかし相手の手の内によっては、それこそが悪手となる恐れもある。　水と火ではないが、陰義によって陰義を封ずるなどという形にはまってしまえば最期だ。
However, depending on the opponent's hand, this could be a bad move. It's not like water to fire, but if it turns out my shinogi was blocked by his shinogi , that would be the end.

敵の手を読めれば良いのだが……　　鬚切か。
It would be great if I could read the enemy's hand... Higekiri, huh.

いつからか、源氏の長たるを証す宝として重んじられてきた名劒冑。　盗賊退治に鬼退治、あるいは獣のように吠えたなど、様々な逸話を持つ。
Since some time or another, it became a renown tsurugi that was honored as a treasure by head of the Minamoto clan. From the extermination of bandits to demons, and its howl that was akin to a beast, it had various anecdotes.

それらを慎重に考察すれば、陰義の正体に当たりをつけることも不可能ではないのだろう。　が、俺の脳内の限られた知識を今の限られた時間で検討してみても、思い当たる何かは無かった。
If I carefully examined them, it would not be impossible to find out the nature of its shinogi. However, even when I tried to go through the limited knowledge I have in my brain, with the limited time I had, I couldn't come up with anything.

刃味の鋭さが特筆されているのは確かなのだが……　どの劒冑の伝説も同じだと言ってしまえばそれまでである。
It is true that the sharpness of the blade is noteworthy... but all tsurugis' legends are the same.

互いに摺り足で位置を移す。　しかし、距離は全く狭まらない。
Both of us shifted our positions. However, the distance does not narrow at all.

焦りは禁物だが……　いつまでも猶予を置くべきではなかった。
We shouldn't be impatient... but we can't stay like this forever.

（良し）
（All right.）

決意する。
I will make up my mind.

「！」


こちらが抜刀の構に移行したのを見て、敵の注意が鋭さを増す。　剣呑なものを感じ取ったに違いない。
The enemy's attention sharpened when he saw that I had shifted to a sword drawing stance.　He must have sensed danger.

――仕掛ける。　但し、半端は抜きで。
――I will make the first move. But this time I won't let it end halfway.

対手の掌中が読めないなら、様子見の一手とゆくのが常道だろうが……むしろ今、それは危険と判断した。　全力死力の一刀で臨む。
If you can't read your opponent's hand, it's usually a good idea to take a wait-and-see approach... But with the current situation, that approach will be more dangerous. I will put my all into one desperate strike.

村正、蒐窮の太刀――電磁抜刀。
Muramasa, the sword of the end―― Railgun.

生半可な術策など打ち砕ける。　この一刀ならば勝負を託せる。
I can get rid of any shallow tricks. This one strike should be able to bring this battle to an end.

「……」
「……」

「……」
「……」

調息し、時を計る。　闇雲な進出は応じ技の餌食。仕掛けるならば相手の出端か、逆に居付いて死に体となった瞬間か。
Take a breath, time it well. Advancing recklessly will just make you fall pre to a counterattack. If you're going to attack, do so when the opponent is about to make their move, or at the moment when they lost their posture.

必ずどちらかの機会は来る。
There will always be an opportunity for one or the other.

どちらだ――――
Which one is it gonna be――――

「……ッ！」
「...Hng!」

合当理?　――また、だと？
The Gattari? Again?

《あれをもう一度やる気なの?》 
《Is he aiming on doing that again?》

（無理だ！）
（That's impossible!）

敵騎の翼甲は傷つき、ほぼ死んでいる。　合当理が健在でも飛べる筈がない。
The enemy's wings are already damaged and nearly dead. There's no way it can fly even if the Gattari is still intact.

何を考えて?
What is he thinking?

「しゃッッ!」
「Shaa!」

「……なっ」
「...Wh」

背を向け――
He turned his back――

逃げる？
He's running away?

「ぐ」
「Guh」

《あ――――っ?》
《Ah-?》

「愚劣!」
「You fool!」

自分に叫んで、俺は跳んだ。
I hurried off as I shouted to myself.

「青いわ、小僧！　戦場に囚われ、戦局を見なかったのう！」
「You're still green, boy! You were so caught up in the battle, you didn't pay attention to the state of the battle!」

嘲笑が耳を打つ。　俺は吐息一つも返せなかった。
His sneer hit my ears. I couldn't even say anything in retort.

（いつの間に――）
（Since when――）

いつの間に。いつの間に。
Since when? Since when?

敵騎は出口を背負っていたのだ?
Since when did he think of dashing to the exit?

鬚切が裏参道へ飛び込む。　わずか、しかし確実に遅れて、俺が続く。
Higekiri flew towards the back path.　I followed, slightly but surely behind.

逃げ道は封じていた――最初の段階では。　敵の曲芸戦術を封じ、追い詰めに掛かった時点でも、唯一の出入口は俺の背後にあった筈だった。
I had sealed off the escape route for the first level. Even as I sealed the enemy's movements and driven him into a corner, the only exit was the one behind me.

それが――いつ！　　……あの間合の取り合いの最中か?
When did he-?! ...Did he do it in the middle of our struggle?

いかにも最後の反撃を企てているように見せかけながら、その実、退路の確保に動いていたのか!
He made it look like he was planning a last-ditch counterattack, but in reality, he was working to secure a way out!

（戦局……！）
（State of battle...!)

その通りだった。　戦闘に没頭し、俺はそれを失念していた。
That was exactly it. I was absorbed in our fight, and I had completely forgot about that.

相手を迅速に仕留める必要があったのは俺だけ。　敵はこの地下空間から生きて逃れさえすれば、勝利条件を満たせるのだ！
I was the only one who needed to finish off my opponent quickly.　As long as the enemy escaped this underground space alive, they could fulfill their victory condition!

それを忘れるとは。
To think that I had forgotten about that.

いや……むしろ忘れなかった大将領が凄まじいのか。　名も知れぬ者に襲われ、命を危うくしている状況で、かくも冷静さを保つとは。
No... rather it's the general who is amazing for not forgetting. It's a good idea to keep your cool when you're in a situation where you're being attacked by someone you don't know and your life is in danger.

これが青二才と古強者の差か。
Is this the difference between a greenhorn and a veteran?

《……地上に出るっ！》
《...He's going to escape to the surface!》

歯軋りするかのような、村正の金打声。
Muramasa's voice sounded as if her teeth were chattering.

間に合わない。　足利護氏を外に出してしまう。
We won't make it. Ashikaga Moriuji is going to escape.

地上では精鋭武者の一団が主君を出迎える。　その守りを破って討つのは……不可能。
On the surface, a band of elite mushas will greet their master. Breaking through their defenses and defeating them is... impossible.

そうなればどうなる。
What will happen if it comes to that?

俺の事はいい。　だが、親王は?
Leaving me aside, what of the prince?

――養父は?
――What about father?

「く……おおっ!」
「

「な」
「W-」

「何だ……これは……」
「What... is this...」

「――――」
「――――」

屍が溢れていた。
There were corpses everywhere.

兵士。　武者。　侍臣。　神官。
Soldiers. Mushas. Attendants. Priests.

地上にいた幕府の人々。八幡宮の人々が。　分け隔てなく、この上もなく平等に、死という同一の運命を享受して在る。
The people of the shogunate who were on the surface. The people on Hachiman shrine.  Equally and indiscriminately, they had all accepted the same fate of death.

生命、存在せず。　静かになだらかに、平穏な世界が現出していた。
There was no life. A world of peace and tranquility had emerged, quietly and gently.

ここは氷原だ。　極北の荒野だ。
This is an ice field.　It's the Arctic wilderness. 

始まりと終わりが共存する。　不動不変の三次元。
The beginning and the end coexist.　Three dimensions that are immovable and unchanging.

《……御堂》
《...Midou》

乾き切った声で、劒冑が俺に注意を促した。
With a dry voice, the tsurugi drew my attention.

視界のほぼ中央。　――貴人を運ぶ牛車が、鎮座している。
Almost in the center of my vision―― An oxcart carrying a nobleman is sitting on the ground.

滑稽なほど場違いな代物。　それを示して、村正が何を告げたいのか、既に痛いほど悟っていた。
A ridiculously out of place article. I was already aware of what Muramasa was trying to say by pointing that out to me.

この光景を見たその刹那に、もうわかっていたのだ。
In that moment of seeing this scene, I already knew.

「……」
「……」

簀垂が揺れる。
The bamboo screen sways.

最初に、白い指先が――　続いて艶やかなる容姿が。　　その奥から現れた。
First, a white fingertip, then a lustrous figure. It appeared from within.

「そなたは……長庚局」
「You are... lady Yuutsuzu.」

「ここで何をしている。何があった。　……そなたの主人はどうした?」
「What are you doing here? What happened? ...What happened to your husband?」

「若宮堂の舞の袖。　静の苧環繰り返し」
「As if pulling a thread from its roll, I would like to go back to those days...」

「返せし人を偲びつつ。　……と」
「when that person would call my name over and over again... or so it goes」

(tl/n: lyrics of folk song "Kamakura". This part of the song tells the story of Yoshitsuaki Gen's concubine, Shizukagozen, who was captured, sent to Kamakura, and was then made to dance in front of Hachiman shrine. I don't know how to translate this part literally without it sounding weird, so I wrote down the meaning behind this part of the song instead. <http://www.worldfolksong.com/songbook/japan/minyo/kamakura.html> )

「すっかり闘戦も果ててからやって来るとは、無粋の謗りを免れまいぞ。　こちらとしても甲斐がない」
「How tactless of you to come right after I've finished my dance. Truly not worth my while.」

「せっかく、よき兵を相手に心楽しく舞えたというのに。　しかし……元より芸とは一輪の花、人目に触れず儚く散るも定めの内というものか」
「Even though I was happily dancing because I had just faced a good opponent. However... I guess art always was akin to a petal of flower, fated to fall without being seen.」

「うむ。花は惜しまず、また咲かせば良い。　今度はおまえを対手として、前にもまさる華やかな舞を演じてくれよう」
「Indeed. There is no need to feel sorry for the flower, we need only to let it bloom once more. This time, with you as my opponent, I will perform an even more spectacular dance than before.」

「嫌とは言うまいな……景明！」
「You wouldn't say no would you, Kageaki?!」

大将領には目もくれず。　その顔貌は真っ直ぐ、俺に向けられた。
She didn't even look at the general. Her face looked straight at me.

光。
Hikaru.

……二年ぶりになる。　生身の姿を、こんなにも近く見るのは。
...It will soon be 2 years, since I've seen her in the flesh so closely. 

その時間、その年頃を思えば意外なほど、光の姿形は記憶の中のそれと違いが少なかった。　俺に一種の失調感を覚えさせるほどであった。
Surprisingly, considering the time and the age, Hikaru's appearance was not so different from the one I remembered.　It was enough to make me feel a kind of ataxia.

何故こんなにも変わりがないのか。　何故こんなにも昔日のままなのか。
Why has so much remained the same?　Why is she still just like how she was back then?

光の運命は、凄烈なまでの変貌を遂げているというのに！
Even though Hikaru's fate is undergoing such a terrible transformation!

「ひか――」
「Hika――」

「応えぬかッ！」
「Are you not going to answer?!」

俺の小声は、別方向の怒声にかき消された。　ん？という顔で光がそちらへ視線を向ける。
My whisper was drowned out by an angry voice from the other direction. Hmm? Hikaru turned her gaze in that direction.

黙殺された格好の大将領であった。
It was the general who was disregarded.

「何か。　急ぎの用件でないなら、家族の対話に割り込まないで頂きたい」
「What? If it's not urgent, I'd appreciate it if you didn't interrupt our family dialogue.」

「……き、　貴様はこの状況が見えておらんのか?」
「...D-Do you not see what's going on?!」

俺の言葉を遮られたことが不興らしい光と、困惑を激昂に繋げつつある六波羅元帥。　両者の世界は悲しいほど隔絶していた。
There was Hikaru who seemed to be displeased that my words were interrupted, as well as general Rokhara who was baffled and filled with fury. Their worlds are so seperated to the point that it's sad.

断崖絶壁の上と下。　　だが――上の光には護氏とそれを取り巻くすべてが見えるが、下の護氏には漠たる空しか見えないのだ。
Like the top and bottom of a precipitous cliff. However―― the one above, Hikaru, could see the general and everything around him, whereas the general below could only see a vague sky.

大将領はいま必要なことを理解していない。
The general doesn't understand what he needs to do now.

「長庚とやら！　この有様の中にいて、何も見ておらぬことはあるまい」
「Yuutsuzu! There is no way you didn't see anything when you're standing in the middle of all this!」

「予の問いに答えよ！　これはいかなる仕儀か?」
「Answer my question! What happened here?!」

「長庚というのはな、世を忍ぶ仮の名だ。　夕暮れの星という意味らしい。人に付けて貰ったものだが、まぁまぁ気に入っている」
「Yuutsuzu is temporary name to hide from this world. It means "star at dusk". It was given to me by someone, and I like it a lot.」

まず俺の方を見て、光は懇切にそう解説した。　それから大将領へ向き直る。
First, Hikaru looked at me and explained in detail. Then she turned to the general.

「おれがやった」
「I was the one who did it.」

「何をだ?」
「Did what?」

「むぅ。　会話になっているようでなっていない」
「Mmm. This doesn't seem like it's going to be a proper conversation.」

何故かわざわざこちらに向かって光は呟いた。
For some reason, Hikaru muttered to us. 

「この者らを斬ったのは誰か、問うたのではないのか？　それがおれだと言っている」
「Did you not ask who killed everyone here? I'm telling you that it was me.」

「……正気か？　貴様」
「...Are you being serious?」

「やにわにその言い草は失敬であろう」
「The way you instantly made that remark is rude.」

「……当然の言葉だ」
「...That's just a natural reaction.」

彼は知らないのだから。　まだ気付いていないのだから。
It's because he doesn't know. He hasn't realized.

「おまえに言われると傷つく……」
「That hurts coming from you...」

「予を愚弄する気かッ！」
「Are you trying to mess with me?!」

「困った。難儀な男だ」
「This is troubling. He's a difficult man.」

《どちらかと言うなら、向こうが正しい気もするのだが》
《If anything, I feel like they're right.》

「なぜだ？」
「Why?」

「貴様がやった、だと……？　夢物語も大概にしろ。貴様の何処にそんな力があると抜かすか！」
「You're saying that you did this...? Take your wild tales elsewhere. How in the world would you have that kind of power to do this?!

「それは無論――」
「Well, naturally that's――」

「…………。　さっきから、おれ一人だけ口が忙しいぞ」
「... Wait, I've been the only one talking a lot for a while.」

《人の相手をいちいち、まめにするからだ。　些事は適当にいなしておけ》
《It's because you always try to take care of everyone's problems. Leave trivial matters aside.》

「むぅ。しかし無礼は好かん。　するのもされるのも」
「Hmm. But I don't like rudeness. Both being rude to someone, and vice versa.」

「貴様、長庚――」
「You, Yuutzusu――」

「……仕方もないな」
「...It can't be helped.」

「先にそっちから済ませることにしよう。　六衛大将領、足利護氏卿」
「I'll take care of you first. General Rikufu, Ashikaga Moriuji.」

「なにィ……？」
「What...?」

「おまえに会いに来た用向はほかでもない。　この光が、覇を問うためだ！」
「I've come to see you for one reason and one reason only.　It is so that I, Hikaru, can ask you about your take on domination!」

ゆるりと伸ばされる腕。　微笑む口元。
An arm stretched out loosely.　A smiling mouth.

紡がれる誓句。
An oath was spun.

「鬼に逢うては鬼を斬る」
「When you meet a demon, slay the demon.」

「仏に逢うては仏を斬る」
「 When you meet Buddha, slay Buddha.」

「……白銀の劒冑……？」
「...A silver tsurugi...?」

「貴様――よもや、」
「Could it be you're-」

「ツルギの理」
「The truth of the tsurugi」

「ここに在り!」
「is here!」

「――銀星号、だと?」
「――the silver star?」

「貴様があの殺戮魔……？　では」
「You're that killer...? Then」

「……では、　貴様を擁していたのは、」
「...then, the one who had you,」

「大将領！　そこらへんの細かいことは後に回せ！」
「General! Save those details for later!」

「おまえは今、己の基を光に問われている」
「Your principles are now being questioned by Hikaru.」

「何……？」
「What...?」

「足利護氏。　天下に武を布かんとする者。光と同じ道を求める者」
「Ashikaga Moriuji. He who seeks to spread war under the heavens. One who seeks the same path as I.」

「覇道の先達に対し、おれは礼節を示そう。　その影を拝して教えを乞おう」
「I shall show civility to my predecessor who also walks the path of Hegemony. I shall bow my head in respect and ask him to teach me.」

「――――」
「――――」

「答えられぬ道理は無かろう」
「There's no reason you shouldn't be able to answer.」

「……はっ。　予とあろう者が、日に二度も下民に大道を問われるとはな！」
「...Haa.　To think that a man of my stature would be asked the same question twice in one day by a lowborn!」

「覇を知りたいか、銀色の化物！」
「You want to know the meaning of domination, you silver monster?!」

「うむ！」
「Yes!」

「ならば知れ！　……奪い取ることだ!」
「Then you shall know! ...It is to take!」

「光?」

「ま、それはそんなに苦労しなかった。　その前の排水溝脱出ゲームに比べればねー」
Well, it wasn't that much trouble. Compared to the drain escape game that came before it.

「……」
「……」

室内に視線を巡らせる。　……いた。
I looked around the room. ...It was there.

枕もとのすぐ近くに、赤い蜘蛛が蹲っている。　身動きもせず。
A red spider is crouched near my pillow. It's not moving.

俺の意識にも反応を示さず。
It's not showing any response even after I'm conscious.

「――――」
「――――」

肝が氷結したのは、一瞬の間の事に過ぎなかった。
The freezing of the liver was something that lasted for an instant.

仕手と劒冑の結縁が教える。　――休眠中だ。
The link between a tsurugi and its master tells me. ――She's inactive.

深い損傷を負ったため、再生以外の全機能を封じて回復に努めているのだろう。　それはそれで無論のこと由々しき事態だが、とりあえず最悪の状態ではない。
She must have been deeply damaged and is trying to recover by shutting down all functions except regeneration. That's a very serious situation, but at any rate, it is not the worst.

俺はほっと息をついた。
I breathed a sigh of relief.

「……ふーん？」
...Hmmm?

「劒冑のこと、心配なんだね」
You're worried about your tsurugi, huh.

「相棒ですから」
She's my partner after all.

「むぅ」
Hmm.

「何か？」
Is something wrong?

「お兄さんのそういう言葉を聞くと、すこしばかりささくれ立つあての胸」
Hearing mister say those words makes my heart tense up a little.

「……何故でしょう」
...And why is that?

「個人的な都合による感情であります。　唐変木め」
It is a feeling due to personal reasons, you impervious man.

「……？」
「……？」

Now then. So, mister. Are you starting to get an idea of who I am and what this place is?

「……」
「……」

「貴方は村正の銘を口にした」
You have spoken the name of Muramasa.

「しましたね」
I did.

「なら貴方は、自分に関わる人間か。　さもなくば」
Then you are a person who is involved with me. Otherwise,

「銀星号に関わる人間という事になります。　……乃至は、その両方に」
that would mean you are a person who is involved with the silver star. ...Perhaps, even both.

「二領しか残ってないもんな。　千子右衛門尉村正の真作は」
Well, there's only two left, aren't there. The genuine works of Sengou Uemon-no-jou Muramasa.

「……」
「……」

And you were there at Hachiman shrine that time.

Yes.

The sword offering ritual―― outsiders were not allowed entry into Hachiman shrine during the progression of such an important ritual.

「そうですね」
That's right.

「……以前から、訝しんでいた事があります。　行方不明者として全国に手配が回っているのに、なぜ光の消息は全く知れないのか」
...I have been wondering about something for a long time.　Why is Hikaru's whereabouts completely unknown when she is being reported as a missing person all over the country?

「二年もの間。　これは、光が誰か有力な人物に保護されている証左なのではないか……と」
For two years. This may be a sign that Hikaru is being protected by someone powerful...

「ごもっとも」
You're right.

...From the room's appearance... I can infer that this is the inside of an impressive mansion.

It's not that impressive. Ah, that's just me being humble. Mister's guess was a bullseye.

Ashikaga Chachamaru of Horigoe Shogunate. I guess I should offer my proper greetings to you, huh.

Mister.

Are you hungry?

Then, let's have breakfast first.

伊豆國、堀越御所。　　庭に面した一間で、朝食の卓と向き合っている。
Horikoshi Palace, Izu Province. In a room facing the garden, I am facing the breakfast table.　　

伊豆半島は山海の幸に恵まれていると聞くが、この品目の多さを見るに、疑念を差し入れる余地は欠片も無さそうであった。　気負いのない自然な膳立てにしてこの彩りは凄い。
I've heard that the Izu Peninsula is blessed with food from the mountains and the sea, but after looking at the variety of items, there seemed to be no room for doubt. The colors of this dish were amazing, and the presentation was natural and unpretentious.

空腹であり、毒飼を危ぶんでいるわけでもないのに――寝顔を晒した後でそんな警戒は馬鹿馬鹿しい――箸の付け所に迷ってしまう。　皿の豊富さにこちらが気負けして、目移りするのだ。
Even though I was hungry and I didn't have to worry about poison―― I mean, it would be silly of me to be that cautious after exposing my sleeping face―― I couldn't decide where I should put my chopsticks. The abundance of dishes is overwhelming and I can't stop looking.

「だからさ、あてとしては言いたいわけよ。　鯨獲るな鯨獲るなって最近にわかに喧しい白人ども、そもそも鯨の数を激減させたのはてめーらじゃねえかってな」
I mean, of course I would want to complain. Those noisy white people recently suddenly told us not to catch whales even though they were the ones who caused the whale population to plummet in the first place.

「大和の捕鯨は生態系まで破壊してねぇ。　大量に獲れるほど船も捕鯨技術も発達してなかったし、一頭獲れば村が半年遊べるってくらい有効に活用してたし」
Our whale fishing is not to the point where it's destroying the ecosystem. The ships and whaling techniques aren't advanced enough to catch large numbers of whales, and even then that system is still effective enough that catching just one is enough for a whole village to play around for half a year.

「そもそも狭い島国の中のこったから需要がそんなになかった。　需要があったのは――世界中の海で獲りに獲ってそれでも足りなかったのは、」
In the first place, since we're in the middle of a small island nation, there's not that much demand for them.  What there was a demand for―― that even hunting in the world's oceans and even then it's still not enough was-

「光源にするんで鯨油が幾らでも必要だったてめーらだろうがぁ！　片脚船長どもの乱獲が鯨を滅ぼしかけてんだよっ!」
whale oil that those guys needed as much as they can get to use for their light sources! Those ahabs' overfishing is destroying the whales!
(tl/n: captain ahab --> fictional character in Moby Dick.) 

「…………」
「…………」

同意も反論も難しい話題であった。
It was a difficult topic to agree or disagree with.

前代大和でも鯨油を光源、また農薬としても用いる需要があり、相当数が獲られた。今世紀に入ってからは南氷洋へ進出し乱獲に加担もしている。　乱獲史の長さで欧州に及ばないのは確かだが……。
Even in the previous Yamato era, there was a demand for whale oil as a source of light and as a pesticide, and a large number of whales were caught. Since the beginning of this century, this has expanded into the Southern Oceans and have contributed to overfishing. It is true that the length of their overfishing history is not as long as Europe's. ...

とりあえず、鯨の佃煮に箸を伸ばす。　旨かった。
For now, I stretched out my chopsticks to eat the whale tsukudani. It was delicious. 

「それが何だオイ。　光源需要がなくなった途端、エコロジーに目覚めやがって」
And then what? As soon as the demand for light sources disappeared, they woke up to ecology.

「絶滅の危機だから保護しましょうだー？　それが自分らの責任を認めて反省するって態度ならまぁ、聞く耳もあるけどさ」
Let's protect them because they're endangered? Although if that's their way of taking responsibility and repentance, then I'll listen.

「あいつら反省なんてカケラもしてねーじゃねえかっ！　てめーの過去は棚に上げて、今のあてらの捕鯨だけ問題にしてぎゃーすか非難しやがる」
But they don't have a shred of remorse! They put their own past on the shelf and just blame the current whaling on us!

「ＮＡ・ＭＥ・Ｎ・ＮＡ!」
DON'T UNDERESTIMATE ME!

「…………」
「…………」

しかしそれは感情的な部分に過ぎない。　肝要の問題は鯨を絶滅から救うことであり、それは確かに実行されなくてはならないだろう……。
But that's just the emotional part. The key issue is to save whales from extinction, and that will certainly have to be done...

内心でそう呟きつつ、鯨の叩きに箸を伸ばす。　旨かった。
I muttered inwardly and stretched out my chopsticks for the whale slices.　It was delicious.

「近頃は連中、鯨は頭のいい動物だから殺すのは野蛮だなんて妙なことまで言ってんな。　アホか。じゃあその鯨の知能を解析して、コミュニケーション取ってこう言ってみろ」
Nowadays, they even say strange things like whales are smart animals and it's barbaric to kill them. Idiots. Then analyze a whale's intelligence, communicate with them and say

「私はあなたの味方ですってな。　賭けてもいいけど、クジラ君はツッコミの衝動を抑えられないと思うぜ」
"I'm on your side". They could try and say that, but I'd wager that whale-kun wouldn't be able to hold back from throwing a punch.

「……確かに、妙な主張ではあります。　知能が高いから殺すなというのは」
...It's a strange argument indeed. To say that we shouldn't kill them because they are intelligent.

「牛や豚は馬鹿だから食ってもいいけど鯨は賢いからだめだってんだからな。　何言ってんのかわかんねー」
You can eat cows and pigs because they're stupid, but you can't eat whales because they're smart. I don't know what they're blabbering about.

「文化の違いから来る思想の違いというものでしょうか」
Is it a difference in thought that comes from cultural differences?

「突き詰めると、人種差別思想が起因かな。　白人的には、優秀な生物はそうでない生物よりも上等って考えは、侵略の歴史を支えてきた馴染み深い正義なんだろ」
When you get right down to it, I guess it comes down to racist thinking. From their of view, the idea that superior creatures are better than less superior creatures is a familiar justice that has supported the history of invasions.

「……成程」
...I see.

鯨の揚物に箸を伸ばしつつ、軽く頷く。　そればかりとは思われないにせよ、一面の真実ではあるかもしれない。揚物は旨かった。
I nodded lightly as I extended my chopsticks to the fried whale.　Even if one would think it's not all that, one thing rings true. The fried food was delicious. 

「ふん、馬鹿くせぇってーの。　あては差別なんかしないもんね。牛も豚も鯨も平等に食う」
Hmph, that's so stupid. I never discriminate. I eat cows, pigs, and whales equally.

「イルカだって食うぞ。　それで思い出したけど一部の大和人がまた腹立つんだよなー。捕鯨は賛成なのにイルカ食うって聞くと『えー』とか言いやがんの」
I even eat dolphins too. This reminds me that some Yamato people are also annoying. They're all for whaling but when they hear that someone eats dolphins, they all go "What~~". 

「イルカ食って悪いかオラ！　つーか鯨はいいけどイルカはだめとか言い出したら捕鯨反対派と同レベルだろーが！」
What's wrong with eating dolphins?! If you say whales are okay but dolphins are not, you're just as bad as the anti-whaling people!

「あてが思うに、奴らは反対派が送り込んだ工作員だな」
My guess is that they're agents sent by the opposition.

「……感情として、イルカ食を受け入れ難いのは理解できます」
...This is just my own feelings, but I understand why it might be hard to accept the thought of eating dolphins.

「捕鯨反対だって感情問題やん。　結局のところ、自分とは違う他人の文化をどう受け止めるかって話だ」
But opposition to whaling is also a matter of feelings. In the end, it's about how you perceive other people's cultures that are different from your own.

「気に食わないからって文句つけるか？　自分とこへ押し売りに来たってんならともかく、よそでやってる分には構わずにおくのが大人の態度ってもんだろ」
Would you complain when you don't like something? It's a different case if someone came to your house to force their products on you, but if they're doing it somewhere else, you leave them alone, that's how adults would behave.

「他文化の尊重。　それは全く同意できます」
Respect for other cultures.　I can totally agree with that.

「でしょーっ？」
Right?

うんうんと頷く堀越公方。　　……さて。前置きの雑談を切るには、いい頃合か。
The Horigoe Shogunate nodded in agreement. ...Now then. It's a good time to end the preamble banter.

Hm, are you done?

Yes. It was a great meal. ...I'd like to get to the point of things, if that's okay.

? What is it?

惚けるかの足利茶々丸を、俺は正面から見据えた。　そうして息を吐き――吸い。

Right now, the silver star is here, correct?

Right now? No she's not.

From what I've heard, it seems the sword offering ceremony is already a thing of three days ago. I must have been asleep for a long time.

そのつもりで自分の身体を点検すれば、成程確かに、寝過ぎた時特有の痛みが随所にある。
When I inspected my body with this in mind, I found that I was indeed experiencing the pain that is typical of sleeping too much.

Please have some teaー

...Thank you very much.

足利茶々丸六波羅中将と二人、縁側に並んで煎茶を啜る。　香りも風味も良い。伊豆は茶の名産地にも近い事を、俺は思い出した。
I'm sipping some sencha on the porch, side by side with the Liutenant General Rokhara, Ashikaga Chachamaru. It has a nice aroma and flavor. I remembered that Izu was also close to a famous tea-producing region.

It's a cloudy day today.

「八幡宮の事件はあての不手際だって言えばそう言えるわけで。　雷蝶あたりから責任追及される前に、先手打って本拠地に自主謹慎したのよ」

銀星号の打撃で吹き飛ばされ――それで死んだにしても生きていたにしても、大将領の体は最終的にあの黒い渦へ呑まれて消えたのであろう。　あれきり姿を現さないなら、そういう事になる。


結果的に舞殿宮の企図は達せられた。　ただ……俺が報告に戻れなかったため、状況を把握するのにさぞ苦労するに違いない。

それは事実なのか。　事実なら何故、そんな事をするのか。


足利茶々丸の目的は何なのか。

多過ぎて、何からどう聞けば良いのかすら悩む。　思いつく端から訊いても良いが――その答えとて、どこまで信用したものなのか……。

光。
